中國電影藝人訪問記（三十四）（續昨） 257

— 沙基

（十四）［奮鬥］導演史東山（下）

［在目前的狀態之下，或是對於政治方面，你有什麽意見沒有？］我說。　　［我覺得無論在何種政治環境之下，對於政治上的錯誤，對於社會的不良，我們在國民立塲上總應當批判和指斥。固然電影應當和政治發生關係，但是要强制電影成爲政治的代言人，到底是極愚笨的方法。因爲這始終是不可能的事。除非電影藝人自身，對於某種政治感覺深切滿意的時候。］

［那末你以爲目前中國需要何種電影？］又是我間。　　［當然，現社會不會使我滿意，所以我以爲極需要暴露社會矛盾的影片。自然這得以事實證明，我個人是反對僅僅是暴露而無指示的影片的。我們應當使觀衆看了電影之後而成爲推動社會的動力。很顯然的，社會有毛病，民衆自身也有毛病。譬如說我們責備不抵抗，但自身更應當拿出抵抗的力量。有許多人常愛獨自坐着說風凉話，這是極不對的態度。……］

在這裏還說了許多，不必一一記載。其次我又說；

［現在我所要知道的是先生對於世界電影的意見了。］

［哼，這個題目很大。不過簡單的說，我以爲最近的俄國電影，的確很有宣傳的力量，他們的電影不僅是一種好玩的東西。英國的電影，近年來大有進步。美國電影，有少數作家在意識上極力掙扎着，力求上進。德國的影片，近來很少，沒有什麽新的意見。總之，各國的電影，都極力提高它自身之地位，而中國電影却不認淸其偉大的力量，眞是可惜。

［再說一句，電影必須以社會的變遷爲轉移，電影必須成爲觀衆所需要的東西。］

說到這裏，我便詢問他今後製片之程序了。他的回答是社會的，民族的相互並重，因爲二者都是目前所急迫需要的東西。譬如這一部［女人］是社會問題的，而下一部將爲民族問題的。其後我又問；

［你入電影以來，已經拍過幾部片子了？］

［這等想一想。］他說：［……哼，一共是十二部了。］

［其中重要的，自己認爲滿意的，可不可以列舉出來？］

［這個麽丨］他用着京戲中道白的調子。

［同性之愛］丨丨民國十四年（二十四歲）

［兒孫福］丨丨丨十五年

［王氏四俠］丨丨十五年

［奇女子］丨丨丨十七年

［姮娘］丨丨丨丨十九年

［奮鬥］丨丨丨丨二十一年（三十一歲）

最後我又問及他入電影界的經過。他的回答是；

［我原是一個學畫的人，好時在春光美術會。後來我因爲和但杜宇是朋友的原故，便在上海影片公司當演員了，其實不過是票友的性質。這是二十歲那一年的事。因爲能够畫畫的原故，間或畫了幾張字幕的佈景，這樣，漸漸的涉及佈景等等。直至二十三歲時，開始導演一部［楊花恨］，那是當時所謂騷姊姊韓雲珍主演的。…以後可以從略了。］

話說到這裏爲止，其他閒話，大可不必詳細記載。這一天，我們談到了社會新聞以至於國家大事，直至下午一時許，方又冒着大雪回家。（十四完）

影片談評

評［展覽會］ 258

— 凌鶴

丨明星出品·新光開映丨

展覽會大半是以［林家舖子］改編的，這是很明顯的事實。當然我們並不要求劇作者完全忠實於小說，因爲文學和電影，在創作過程中，有着極大的差異。但是這［展覽會］和原著之問，却是完全變了原質的東西，特别是在恊昌源（林家舖子）洋貨店倒閉之後，再加上一段原著所未有的［提倡國貨］，［展覽會］等等，却完全和整個的主旨相反了。我以爲這是最不聰明的方法。至於其他許多廢　了原作本意的地方，那當然是另一問題了。

農村破産，購買力减低，間接直接的敲詐剝削，商人之間的陰謀暗鬥，時事不靖，金融恐慌，商家的週轉不靈，小資本的商店，只有極凄慘的倒閉，這是最顯著而無可避免的事實。同時，在原著上也得明白的寫出：［不毁纔是作怪………老爺敲詐他，錢莊壓迫他，同業又中傷他，而又要吃倒賬，憑誰也受不了這樣重重的折磨罷？……］

這些，在電影上都以極晦澀的手法，相當的說了出來。但是，在後面劇作者突然加上一個莫明其妙的尾巴，其苦口婆戊的提倡國貨的精神，固在可嘉，可是在［展覽會］中却是極不通的矛盾了。他如恊昌源倒閉之後，那對門一家作惡多端的湧盛祥也跟着倒閉，說是受了恊昌源的影響，也是不能自圓其說的地方，這完全是怯弱的爲了迎合觀衆封建的旣成心理，而來一個天理昭彰的果報。當然，我們並不說湧盛祥還可獨存於這不景氣的年頭，但是爲了大快人心，又不能說出更好的理由。却不能不使人責難了。假使說，就在趙老闆逃走之後，他的生産被拍賣分攤；這一悲劇的收塲，不是更能加深商人們之刺激嗎？

導演的手法，我們不能忘記他在［香草美人］中相當的成功。但是在這一影片中，他却完全失敗了。

㈠我們不能很顯然的分出，那一家是湧盛祥，那一家是恊昌源，有時竟糊糊塗塗的以甲爲乙。這使我們想起華納出品的［生意經］，同樣是兩家對門的商店；眞是差得太遠了。

㈡劇中沒有感情，連一點幽鬱的空氣，都沒有很好的把握着。我以爲這是使觀衆最感覺掃興的地方。、

㈢佈景太簡單而且太假，雪以棉花白粉，紙片做成，這不是有意使人嘆氣麽？

㈣演員無戲可做，尤其是孫敏和王夢石他們，簡直只是一點細微的點綴。比較好的，當然還是謝雲卿，高逸安二人。王徵信次之，夏佩珍又次之，至於一位穿黑絨馬褂，以水烟袋爲裝飾品的飾錢莊老闆的，却眞敎人噴飯了。

㈤化裝太假，尤其是那位錢莊老闆。謝雲卿有幾塲也是同樣，我眞不懂爲什麽如此不愼重？

總之，這是明星公司水平綫下的作品。

紀念金傳松君 259

金傳松君本爲聯華二廠電氣部之工友，亦卽是我們電影文化運動中的一個優秀而刻苦的技術人員。他在一九三三年末參加蔡楚生君導演的［漁光曲］一片工作時，在攝影塲偶爲洋釘刺傷足部，創口潰爛終於本年一月十日在體育醫院身故，爲紀念我們喪失了一位忠實同志的哀忱，我們經於本月十四日在聯華二廠俱樂部舉行追悼大會，在會中我們特别，對於金君在受傷後依舊獨力，爰助工作之精神表示我們最大之致意，引爲我們每一位同仁今後工作的模範，並指出以後應從廠内醫藥設備之改善以及同仁間密切互助精神之發揮，才足以减少不幸事件之再現，同時爲紀念金君之偉大工作精神議决在二廠内樹立銅牌永懸紀念。最後由同仁發起善後募捐以維持金君老母之暮年而金君身後種種善後措置亦由大會委託同仁會中服務部中專責妥爲辦理。

銀幕大情侶蓋諾法雷合作先聲 260

— 阿韻

在過去一年中，珍妮蓋諾和却爾斯法雷的不合作問題，是震驚銀壇的一件大變動，甚至於法雷自動解除合同，脫離了福斯公司，對他們倆有相當好感的，都表示相當的惋惜。但據最近福斯公司正式的宣佈，蓋諾法雷再度搭擋，繼續合作兩部片，已經正式訂立合同了。在想望了好久的全世界影迷，誠然是較可喜的事實。就在法雷自己，也很想在再度合作中，掙扎出一個新形式，新自我來。所以，在合同訂立的事前，特别提出一條劇本有權取捨，要合乎他的調性，要有相當做戲的機會，他决不再是蓋諾的附屬品，他要全世界觀衆了解他是個富有個性的一員，並不是憑藉蓋諾的表演而倖致他聲名的。第一部片已在本月初開始工作，片名還沒有正式宣佈

却利卓别靈和德國總理希特勒 261

— 思瀛

美國電影雜誌裏面，帶着滑稽口吻地說：希特勒的部下要和却利卓别靈勢不兩立了，其原因就是因爲這位笑匠的小鬍子，和德國堂堂總理，國家社會黨的領袖，希特勒氏的小鬍子，太不分上下高低了。又有人說却利自己不願保留那個小鬍子了，因爲恐怕被人家誤認爲希特勒。又有人說德國的國家社會黨已經向却利要求剃去他的小鬍子，因爲他那可笑的小鬍子，顯然他與他們的首領開玩笑了。但是我們要知道，却利的小鬍子，不是從今天帶起的。遠在希特勒的大名，被人家知道以前，這位笑匠早已用那小鬍子，大皮靴和手杖做他的商標了。依據商標法，希特勒還是冒牌哩！但是很顯然的一件事，就是却利卓别靈的片子，恐怕難以進德國的領土了。

電影小說

婆心劇盜Ｂｒｏａｄｗａｙ　Ｔｈｒｕ　ａ　Ｋｅｙｈｏｌｅ（二） 262

— 信之

審判官李琪道：［什麽？祗有你才配那個花，因爲你自己比白玉蘭還要美麗。不過你還沒有看見花裏面包的東西哩。］瓊看見那紥花的當中，有一個小包裹，她要去拿了。李琪連忙欄阻道：［孩子，且别動，現在還沒有到時候。等到你到了你的化妝室，再打開看好了。］瓊嬌笑着：［無論那是什麽，總之太好了。］她說完了，就捧着花回她的化妝室去了。

瓊蕙蘭回到化妝室，泰克絲正在那裏。她將那小包裹折開了，裏面發現了一副鑽石鑲嵌的手鐲。瓊蕙蘭興高彩烈地喊道：［泰克絲，你來看，這是什麽！審判官李琪送給我的！這個東西眞好看丨丨但是我當然不能接受它的。］泰克絲將那付手鐲仔細地估騐了一下，然後還給瓊蕙蘭道：［喂，瓊，你在這種地方，還是沒有出道，但是你是很有出息的。所以我要告訴你，你知道人家都說世界上每一分鐘，一定有一個傻子降生，但是事實上，却大大不然。傻子並不多而是很難遇見的。並且，你聽見過有人中了白金的毒死的沒有］？她說定了，將片己的胳膊伸了出來，看着滿胳膊的手鐲說道：［這些東西等到我年紀大了，是極有用塲的。你要記得，這些東西怎麽得來的，不是將頭左右擺着可以將來的，是要將頭上下點着才興哩。］現在你還想拿那付手鐲還給那東西的嗎？］瓊蕙蘭道：［當然，我是應黨還給他的。］泰克絲摇摇頭，表示著絕望的神氣走開了。

瓊蕙蘭說的是實話，她說她並不認識那介紹她到這個夜總會來的弗蘭克羅其。羅其是個有名的壞東西，而泰克斯喀萊，亦不是個好東西。當然她開設的夜總會，不是個甚麽名譽的地方了。瓊蕙蘭還記得她的小時候，弗蘭克是她姊姊的朋友。那時候大家已經知道弗蘭克是隣近一帶的壞孩子。後來又聽見人家說，他加入了一個强盜黨了。但是她始終還有知道他現在已經變成了紐約最可怕的一個盜魁了。他做的是什麽事呢？他是一個［鷄鴨保險會］的會長，凡紐約一帶的鷄鴨商人，都要按照他們做營業的大小，向茀蘭克羅其繳納一個保護稅，才可以將他們的商品，安全送到他們主顧的家裏。瓊蕙蘭的姊姊伊塞爾，託了他將她的妹妹薦到一個戲院裏去學習。在泰克絲的夜總會裏，羅其的話就是法律，因此瓊蕙蘭就被送到這裹來作一個歌女。有一天羅其和他的隨身護衛查克，和查克和女人　别兒，一同來到夜總會裏來看那兒的表演。他漸漸地注意到那一排女子的最未一個。泰克絲這時正巧走了過來。（未完）

1934.01.22

Generals of the Nineteenth Route Army Send Telegram Supporting the Central Government 1

Central Army Enters Zhangzhou Successively, Chiang Ting-wen Arrives in Xiamen

Rumor Has It Chen Jitang Has Ordered Guangdong Troops to Cease Entering Fujian

(Xiamen) Quanzhou Dispatch: Quanzhou City was recovered at 12:00 PM on the 21st. The whole city is flying the Blue Sky White Sun national flag and is stable. Chiang Ting-wen arrived in Xiamen from the provincial capital by plane at 12:00 PM on the 21st. He landed at the airport and immediately went to the commander's office at Ji 囗囗 to supervise the troops. The headquarters of the 3rd Division is located at Songyu. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Military News: The 3rd Division recovered most of Zhangzhou at 12:00 PM on the 21st. They moved from Jiaowei towards Tong'an, and there was news that the county seat was taken at 12:00 PM. This was mainly because the Central Army attacked Xianyou very urgently from the south, and the 19th Route Army was in a tight encirclement, so the matter was quickly resolved. Also, Yang Fengnian recently announced that Yang Sanhua, a separate detachment of the Anti-Rebel Army, captured Zhangzhou on the morning of the 21st and entered the city completely. Also, military report: the 3rd Division's replenishment regiment entered Zhangzhou at 2:00 PM. The enemy had already retreated the night before. Chiang Ting-wen flew to Xiamen by plane at 4:30 PM, escorted by three aircraft. After Chiang arrived, he stayed at Du Qiyun's special envoy office. The Anti-Rebel Army captured Tong'an at 12:00 PM on the 21st. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Quanzhou Telegram: Shen Mao and others telegraphed their defection on the 21st and telegraphed to Hong Kong to welcome Dai Zai. Cai left Quanzhou on the morning of the 21st. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) At 2:00 PM on the 21st, the generals of the 19th Route Army sent a telegram to the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, the National Government, and the Military Affairs Commission. The telegram was led by Shen Guanghan, stating that Guanghan and others had decided to break away from the People's Government, support the Central Government, urge Li, Chen, Jiang, and Cai to leave first, and recommend Comrade Dai Ji to take over the maintenance. All political issues will be resolved later through discussion. In addition to ordering the troops to assemble and cease military action, awaiting peaceful resolution, they respectfully inform Shen Han, commander of the 60th Division of the 19th Army, Mao Weishou, commander of the 61st Division, Qu Shounian, commander of the 78th Division, Zhang Yan, commander of the 49th Division, and all officers and soldiers. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) The Central Army arrived in Xiamen to attack Zhangzhou. The 囗 brigade and 囗 brigade of the □ Division were transported from the provincial capital to Xiamen on six merchant ships, including the "Tai Shun," on the morning of the 20th. They docked behind Gulangyu and landed at Songyu Fugong at 11:00 AM, approximately 10,000 people. Two routes advanced towards Zhangzhou. Li himself supervised the troops. One route to Songyu arrived at Jiangdong Bridge in the evening, only thirty *li* from Zhangzhou. The 19th Route Army stationed in Zhangzhou had only one regiment, and upon hearing the news, they immediately retreated west of Zhangzhou. The Central Army could completely occupy Zhangzhou on the evening of the 21st. Chen Mingshu and Li Jishen left Zhangzhou by plane at 12:00 PM on the 20th, reportedly flying to Quanzhou. Cai Tingkai and Jiang Guangnai were in Quanzhou. Most of the 19th Route Army gathered in Xingquan. The Central Army crossed the Wulong River south on the 17th to pursue and arrived at Xianyou on the 19th, attacking the remnants of the 19th Route Army in Quanzhou. On the 21st, □ Division still had two regiments arriving in Xiamen and entering Zhangzhou to completely resolve the Fujian situation. The Guangdong troops had just arrived at the Fujian border. According to Shantou news on the 20th, Chen Jitang had ordered the cessation of entry into Fujian. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Military News: Two divisions of the Central Army can continue to arrive in Xiamen on the 21st. One division landed and entered Zhangzhou, and the other landed at the old town of Zhangpu, preparing to open up the Yunxiao Guangdong border area. The 4th and 5th detachments of Yang Fengnian's Anti-Rebel Army in southern Fujian captured Pinghe and Yongding on the 18th. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Xiamen) Military News: Over 3,000 Quan-Yong people's army, reorganized by Weng Zhaoyuan, defected in Yongchun Dehua. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) The majority of the rebel army retreated south, passing through Yongtai. Our army is tracking and pursuing them. Also, our units advancing south from Shaxi are flanking and attacking Zhangzhou and Quanzhou from the east. (21st Special Dispatch)

Zhangzhou Garrison Surrenders Without a Fight 2

(Xiamen) This morning, eight warships dispatched a large number of troops to land on the land opposite Xiamen and advance towards Zhangzhou. This afternoon, the Zhangzhou garrison surrendered without a fight. The remaining forces of the rebel army in Fujian province no longer have any chance of revival. (21st Reuters Dispatch)

Songyu and Jiaowei Recovered 3

(Nanchang) The Forward Headquarters has just received a telegram stating that our army has recovered Songyu and Jiaowei, opposite Xiamen. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Guangdong Side to Plan Entire Strategy 4

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang has scheduled a meeting of all returning provincial generals for the 22nd to discuss the entire military plan for Fujian. Chen Jitang sent Miao Peinan to inspect the Dongjiang River, departing this week. Li Hanfun returned to Shaozhou on the 21st. Yu Moumou sent Yang Zhuoxiu back to the province on the 21st to report on defense matters. (21st Special Dispatch)

Nineteenth Route Army Ceases Recruiting New Soldiers 5

(Hong Kong) The Nineteenth Route Army previously sent personnel to Guangxi to recruit soldiers but has now automatically ceased recruitment. (21st Special Dispatch)

Anti-Guangdong Sentiment Erupts in Fuzhou and Xiamen 6

(Hong Kong) Chen Wei-yuan, the Guangdong Military Commissioner for Southern Fujian, has entered Fujian. Guangdong people traveling in Fuzhou and Xiamen are returning to Guangdong to temporarily take shelter due to the anti-Guangdong sentiment that has erupted there. (21st Special Dispatch)

Naval Academy Prepares to Move Back to Mawei 7

(Nanjing) The Naval Academy is moving all naval organizations back to Mawei to the original school on the 25th for classes because order has been restored in Fuzhou. (21st Special Dispatch)

People's Militia in Southern Fujian Respond to the Central Government 8

(Nanjing) Song Yuanyuan, special envoy for Fujian pacification, said that after the rebel army retreated to southern Fujian, most gathered in Putian Hanjiang, while the rest were divided to guard Hui'an, Quanzhou, Tong'an, Zhangzhou, and other places, with a defense line of over 600 *li*, putting them in a most unfavorable position. The people's militia in southern Fujian are now being contacted by Yang Fengnian, Yu Chengyao, Gao Yi, Xu Ruilin, and others, and they have all launched a response to the Central Government. Among them, Yu Chengyao's Xingquan Anti-Rebel Army, reorganized from Weng Zhaoyuan's People's Self-Defense Army, totals over 10,000 men. Originally stationed in Yongtai, Dehua, Xianyou, Nan'an, Anxi, and other counties, they have made contact with the Central Army that arrived in Yongtai and Xianyou, cutting off the rebel army's transportation. Yang, Gao, Xu, and other units can also cut off their transportation in the Zhangnan area. Although the Nineteenth Route Army still has over 20,000 men retreating to southern Fujian, they are cut into several sections and can all be eliminated. The Guangdong troops have recently moved to the Fujian border, intending to reorganize the Nineteenth Route Army, but they are over 200 *li* away from the Fujian border, with Yang Fengnian's unit intercepting them in the Xiaoxi Shancheng area of Zhangpu. Even if the rebel army wants to flee to Guangdong, it will be difficult to pass through. (21st Special Dispatch)

Chen Yi's Date of Departure for Fujian Undecided 9

(Nanjing) Chen Yi's date of departure for Fujian will be determined after seeking instructions from Chiang. As for the selection of personnel for the Fujian provincial committee, it will also be decided at that time. (21st Special Dispatch)

Fang Shengtao Discusses Military Affairs in Southern Fujian 10

(Nanjing) Fang Shengtao has returned to Nanjing after inspecting the northern Fujian area. His old illness has recurred, and he is currently receiving medical treatment. Fang said that the aftermath of the Fujian situation is complicated. The Central Government has appointed Chen Yi as chairman, and after the provincial government is organized, there will be relief measures. Although the rebel army has now retreated to the Zhangquan area of southern Fujian, the provincial defense forces in that area are strong. The provincial defense in northern Fujian has now been reorganized into the Northern Fujian Anti-Rebel Army, with two brigades. The southern Fujian provincial defense army has also been reorganized into the Southern Fujian Anti-Rebel Army, with a commander-in-chief and a deputy commander, commanding even more troops than in northern Fujian. Moreover, the provincial defense forces are familiar with the geography. The 19th Army cannot fight and the province will be completely cleared out of question. (21st Special Dispatch)

Navy Temporarily Maintains Security in Fujian 11

(Nanjing) Navy Chief Chen Shaokuan went to Fujian to command the navy and recover Fujian. He returned to Shanghai and transferred to Nanjing by the Ninghai warship. He said that after this departure, he first went to Sandu to consult with the commanders of various fleets on strategy, and then led the team to Fuzhou. Under our pressure, the rebel army resisted slightly and then collapsed. The provincial capital was then recovered. Because the Fujian provincial government has not yet been established, the commander of the First Fleet, Chen Jiliang, is stationed to maintain security. Once the new chairman Chen Yi arrives in Fujian and the provincial government is established, Commander Chen will lead the Marine Corps out of the provincial capital, and Chen will return to Shanghai to be stationed. The 19th Route Army has lost more than half of its strength this time, and is internally divided, and has no more combat capability. Chen Mingshu and Li Jishen are still obsessed and are still in Zhangzhou, intending to survive. Our frontline has passed Putian and Xianyou. According to my prediction, Zhangquan can be completely recovered in two or three days, and the campaign against Fujian can be completely concluded within a week. Reuters previously reported that the rebel army was reorganizing its remnants in Zhangzhou and other places, and wanted to attack Xiamen again, but that has now passed. The rebel side knows that the naval fleet and marine corps in Xiamen are very strictly deployed, and they dare not peep. Lin Guogeng, the commander of Xiamen's main port, is responsible for security and will also restore normalcy. This time, the entire navy fleet fought fiercely with the rebel army one after another, consuming a lot of ammunition. The details have not yet been calculated. The losses of naval agencies and buildings in various places in Fujian are about five to six hundred thousand, and repairs are underway. However, major repairs require too much money and are awaiting government appropriation. The details of the losses have been reported to the government for record. (21st Special Dispatch)

Putian County Seat Has Been Recovered 12

(Nanjing) Military News: According to a telegram from Putian, a certain division of the Central Army occupied Putian County at 12:00 PM on the 20th. Two regiments of Zhang Yan's rebel troops were disarmed by us, and countless ammunition and baggage were seized. The entire rebel force has been eliminated. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Sa Zhenbing Organizes Maintenance Committee 13

(Fuzhou) On the afternoon of the 15th, Sa Zhenbing issued a notice in the name of the chairman of the Security Maintenance Committee, stating that Zhenbing's feelings are related to his hometown and he cannot refuse his duty. He immediately hired Public Security Bureau Chief Qiu Guozhen, Chamber of Commerce Luo Mianhou, Fire Association President Wang Gang, and diplomat Wang Shichang as members to organize and establish the committee that day, working at the Public Security Bureau. (16th Special Dispatch)

Shen Guanghan and Others Break Away From the Puppet Government 14

(Fuzhou) Shen Guanghan, Mao Weishou, Qu Shounian, Zhang Yan, and others telegraphed on the 21st to break away from the puppet government and support the Central Government. The original telegram stated that Guanghan and others had decided to unanimously break away from the puppet government, support the Central Government, and protect the peace of the country. They hoped that all enlightened people in the country would express their sympathy. In addition to ordering all troops to assemble and cease military action, awaiting processing, they respectfully informed, etc. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Mao and Zhang Prepare to Expel Chen and Li 15

(Hong Kong) Mao Weishou and Zhang Yan are preparing to expel Chen and Li. They have secretly sent representatives to Hong Kong to invite Dai Zai to enter Fujian and take over the remnants of the army. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

The Order of the Presidium and the Agenda Have Been Decided

Preparatory Meeting After Memorial Week, Group Reviews of Proposals in the Afternoon

Secretariat of the Congress Intensifies Work

It is Said That the Formal Meeting Will Be Held Immediately After Memorial Week

(Nanjing) The Presidium of the Fourth Plenary Session held a meeting on the morning of the 21st to decide the procedures for discussing proposals at the congress and the order of rotation of the chairmen. It is reported that it has been drafted. The chairman of the first congress is Chiang Kai-shek, the second is Wang, the third is Sun, the fourth is Yu, the fifth is Ju, the sixth is Dai, the seventh is Gu, and so on in rotation. According to a certain committee member, today is the weekly holiday, and all committee members in Nanjing are exchanging opinions. The Secretariat of the Congress is busy with work and is still working as usual, even on the holiday, and has stipulated that the deadline for accepting proposals is the 23rd. The Congress was originally scheduled to hold a preparatory meeting again tomorrow morning, but to save time, it is proposed to hold the formal meeting immediately after the expanded memorial week tomorrow. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Presidium of the Plenary Session held a meeting at Wang's residence in Luyuan New Village at 9:00 AM on the morning of the 21st. In addition to Chiang Kai-shek, Wang Zhaoming, Sun Ke, Dai Chuanxian, Yu Youren, Gu Mengyu, Ju Zheng, and six

committee members participated. Decisions were made on the order of the congress chairman and the agenda. The order of the congress chairman will be based on the order elected at the preparatory meeting. The deadline for receiving proposals is the 23rd. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Southwestern Proposals Are Not Serious 20

(Nanjing) Cui Guangxiu said that the southwestern proposals, in addition to being jointly signed by more than a dozen Central Committee members in Guangdong, were also jointly signed by Cheng Qian, Chen Jiayou, He Shizhen, Chen Zhongfu, Yang Shukan, and others after arriving in Shanghai. Zhang Zhiben, Sun Jingya, and others in Nanjing also jointly signed it. The committee members of Wang Jingwei and Sun Zhesheng will also be asked to co-sign the documents. Cui continued, "Although the content of the proposals is based on Hu Zhantang's eight demands, it is definitely not as exaggerated as reported by the outside world. These demands of Mr. Hu are also what the responsible persons of the Central Government have vigorously advocated in the past. Now that the southwestern committee members have re-submitted them, it is only to promote their implementation. Moreover, the opinions of the southwestern committee members are directed at the matter and not at the person. For example, in the political field, they only say how the political system should meet the needs, and there is no contention over positions." As for whether Mr. Hu will come to Nanjing to jointly shoulder the major responsibilities of the party and the country, he has not heard of it. Huang Xuchu, a central committee member from Guangxi province, left later than I did, and will arrive tomorrow morning, he said. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Miao Bin, a member of the review committee of the plenary session's political group, said that he has not seen the full picture of the southwestern proposal, so he cannot participate in the opinions. However, he heard that this case is based on Mr. Hu's principles. If it is beneficial to the party, it can be carefully reviewed and kept secret. (21st Special Dispatch)

Japan Will Dispatch Special Representative

To Celebrate the Ascent of the Puppet 25

Pu Yi Plans to Go to Japan in Person to Express Gratitude

The United States is Extremely Pessimistic About the Far East

(Tokyo) When Pu Yi holds his enthronement ceremony in Changchun on March 1st, the Japanese side will, as usual, have representatives from the Manchurian institutions, including Ambassador Hishikari, attend. However, since this is the greatest event marking a new era for [Manchukuo], there is a proposal to dispatch a prominent figure as a special representative to participate at the same time as Ambassador Hishikari, to express the greatest congratulations on the implementation of the [Manchukuo] imperial system. The relevant authorities are currently negotiating, and it can be formally specified within the next few days. (21st Dentong Telegram)

The cost is 331,500 Japanese yen and has been included in the grand ceremony budget. (21st Dentong News Agency Telegram)

(Washington) Important officials here are paying close attention to Pu Yi's recent proclamation of himself as emperor in [Manchukuo]. At a press conference with reporters from the New Voice today, they stated that the change of [Manchukuo] to an empire and the establishment of a new political system do not pose major problems for relations with Russia, but they are closely related to the interests of the United States. Although the US government still does not want to express any opinions, it is extremely pessimistic about the situation in the Far East, saying that it is like an arrow on a string, ready to be launched at any moment. (20th National Telegram)

(Tokyo) What will be the attitude and policy of the Japanese army towards [Manchukuo] after the implementation of the imperial system? Naturally, it will be even more respectful to the [Emperor], and its guidance and assistance to [Manchukuo] will remain the same as before. (21st Dentong Telegram)

Liu Zhenhua and Li Fulin Also Arrive in Nanjing

In addition to attending the Fourth Plenary Session, he is also reporting the recent situation in North China to the Military Sub-Committee and the Central Committee on behalf of He. Regarding the reception of Yuguan, both sides have reached an understanding and are expected to receive it soon. After the rebellion of Liu Guitang's troops, over 2,000 of his cavalry fled to the border between Hebei and Shandong, and are currently being jointly suppressed by the three provinces of Hebei, Chahar, and Shandong. Huang Fu Visits the Panchen Lama 28

Chairman Lin Welcomes Representatives to Peiping

(Peiping) The Panchen Lama is scheduled to go to Nanjing tomorrow to attend the Fourth Plenary Session. Huang Fu visited the Panchen Lama this morning and talked for a long time. (21st Special Dispatch) (Peiping) Lin Xiang, who was sent by Chairman Lin to Peiping to welcome the Panchen Lama, arrived in Peiping this afternoon and immediately went to Jurentang to visit He. Later, he went to Fengzeyuan to visit the Panchen Lama and presented a personal letter from Lin Dai, welcoming him to Nanjing as soon as possible. The Panchen Lama said that he will be to Nanjing on the 22nd. (21st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Panchen Lama's office in Nanjing received a telegram from Peiping stating that the Panchen Lama is scheduled to come to Nanjing from Peiping on the 22nd and will arrive on the 24th. (21st Central News Agency Telegram)

(Peiping) The Panchen Lama is scheduled to go to Nanjing on the 22nd. Today, he telegraphed Wang, Dai, and Shi Qingyang, reporting his itinerary. The Panchen Lama will stay in Nanjing for two months before returning north and entering the Yikezhao League. He has sent Ma Kanbu and over 20 others to the Yikezhao League to prepare everything. The date of entering Tibet must be determined after Huang Musong's visit to Tibet to express condolences yields results, and then he and the Central Committee will discuss the matter in detail. Current Commentary

The Impact of the British, American, and French Exchange Rate War 30

In order to save the American economy from panic, US President Roosevelt proposed a currency bill to the Senate and House of Representatives on the 15th of this month. The main points of the content are three. The first is to lower the pure gold content of American currency. The second is for the Ministry of Finance to take over approximately 40 billion *yuan* (par value) of gold stored in the Federal Reserve Banks. The third is to set up an exchange rate stabilization fund of approximately 20 billion *yuan*. The American authorities believe that if the bill can be implemented, it will definitely be enough to raise prices, lower exchange rates, and restore prosperity. Without this, it will be insufficient to achieve success. However, from our observation, the so-called goal of raising prices may not be realized. Even the manipulation of exchange rates may only intensify the opposition of international relations and promote the rapid progress of economic control. Therefore, at a time when the panic of war preparation is becoming increasingly urgent, Roosevelt's policy can be said to be a representation of the United States' economic arming and advance deployment. The repercussions caused by this are not to be ignored.

According to the Havas Washington telegram of the 18th, Roosevelt's currency plan has now passed the House Monetary Committee by a vote of fifteen to one. At the same time, the committee stated that "the government is using 20 billion *yuan* as a fund to stabilize exchange rates, and its purpose is to prevent the exchange rate of American currency from being threatened by the UK and France again. The United States should have the right to self-defense, etc." From this, it can be seen that the reason why the United States is rushing to manage the nation's gold is partly to cope with the power of the UK and France to manipulate exchange rates, but more importantly to protect the original market of the United States overseas. The economic panic of the US in the recent years has caused huge losses. It is certainly in the same boat as the UK and France. However, France from the beginning dug deep trenches and built high barriers, strictly constructing tax walls. The UK and Japan also successively lowered currency prices and strictly manipulated exchange rates. The result was a major blow to the overseas markets of the United States. Since Roosevelt took office, he reversed President Hoover's actions, first stopping the use of the gold standard, and then following up with a large-scale gold purchase policy. If that was not enough, he followed up with the current plan to concentrate gold and control exchange rates, believing that in such a shift, huge profits could be obtained. Setting up a stabilization fund of 20 billion *yuan* is equivalent to France's huge amount of gold and the UK's stabilization fund of 350 million pounds. The world's exchange market is also worthy of competing with various powers. However, the agility and combativeness of the UK and France cannot be underestimated.

Looking at the serious repercussions that have been stirred up in London and Paris since Roosevelt's currency plan was proposed. The exchange rate of silver dollars in this city against the UK, US, and Japan has also consistently tended to fall. The fall in the currency prices of these countries shows that the fierce exchange rate war is already leaping up rapidly. Although there is still some debate within the US Congress, it is not legal for the government to take over the gold of the Reserve Banks, but there is no disagreement in principle regarding the reduction of the pure gold content of the US dollar, the confiscation of the depreciation benefits of the US dollar, and the establishment of a stabilization fund. The US is struggling from the shock of economic panic, and without this, it will be insufficient to make an effort. The UK, France, and other countries are doing this because it is the only way to cope with their markets. This is a necessary trend in the exchange rate war. However, as a weak country with rising foreign exchange rates, the rampant import of foreign goods is becoming more and more serious. In such an economic frenzy, how can we seek economic self-defense?

Our reporter in Tianjin

Zhu Xiaofu Dies of Serious Injuries 31

(Beiping) Our Tianjin correspondent Zhu Xiaofu was shot by robbers last night and died of serious injuries. He passed away this morning. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Our correspondent Zhu Xiaofu passed away at the hospital at 9 AM on the 21st. He was dressed in accordance with religious rites that day and moved into a mosque. The funeral is scheduled for the 23rd, and he will be temporarily buried in a public cemetery. (21st Dispatch)

(Tianjin) At the private residence of our Tianjin correspondent Zhu Xiaofu in Hongyin Lane, French Concession, Tianjin, at around 6 PM on the 20th, four thugs suddenly broke in, robbed him of fur coats and other items, and shot Zhu in the face with a pistol as they were leaving. Zhu immediately fell to the ground, and the bandits escaped. After a female servant reported to the police, Zhu was sent to the French Hospital for treatment, but he died of excessive blood loss at 8 AM on the 21st. The court's inspection office sent personnel to the hospital to examine the body. Zhu had served in the Tianjin press for many years and left behind a sister and a son, leaving his family in dire straits. In addition, the French Municipal Council has been investigating the case and has found clues. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

Ma Hongkui's telegram stated

Sun's Army Surrounds Pingluo 32

Sun Dianying Asks the Central Government to Send Personnel to Supervise the Departure

Zhu Shaoliang Telegram Urges Sun to Quickly Withdraw from Dengkou

The Military Commission Plans to Resolve the Sun-Ma Conflict

(Beiping) Ma Hongbin and Ma Hongkui sent two telegrams to He Yingqin this morning. One telegram stated: "I have just received a report from Ma Binlin, the brigade commander stationed in Pingluo, at 8:00 PM on the 20th, stating that enemy troops surrounded Pingluo on the east, west, and north sides after 5:00 PM on the 19th, and launched a pincer attack that night. From 4:00 to 6:00 AM this morning, they bombarded heavily. Our officers and soldiers remained calm and alert and did not retaliate. I am determined to coexist with this city," etc. I ordered them to remain calm and hold firm, awaiting orders to attack. The other telegram stated: "I have just received a report from Ma Binlin, the brigade commander stationed in Pingluo, stating that at 5:00 PM today, Sun's infantry took a three-sided encirclement of Pingluo, and the enemy on the north side has begun a pincer attack," etc. Also, according to a report from Hao Jinyuan, the battalion commander stationed in Hongguangying, "At 7:00 PM today, Yang Houxiaozi's cavalry and Wang Suiqing's special service regiment are approaching the city, intending to attack Pingluo tonight to join forces with Yu Shiming's cavalry to attack Ligangbao," etc. It is clear that Sun's army is defying orders, resorting to arms, and attacking Ningxia, and there is no way to conceal it. Yet, they claim that my troops are blocking them and provoking them. This kind of trick of burying one's head in the sand cannot hide the truth from the world. For the sake of legitimate self-defense, I have ordered all units to prepare for war." (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Ma Hongbin and Ma Hongkui sent a telegram to He Yingqin at 2:00 PM on the 19th, stating that Yu Shiming gave the order to the army to attack Ligangbao from Woye at 2:00 PM on the 16th of this month. The original text is very long. (21st Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Dianying telegraphed Wang Shiping, stating, "This time, the troops of my army stationed in the Sanshenggong area of Dengkou must pass through Shizuizi in Woye. Ma cannot understand and sent troops to intercept. He Yingqin telegraphed to stop, and I have ordered the troops advancing to Shizuizi to stop. As for the troops defending Wuyuan and Linhe, they are turning to Woye from the east bank of the river in Suiyuan. Ma again claimed that Woye is under the jurisdiction of Ningxia and sent troops to intercept, forbidding them to go to Woye. Woye originally belonged to the Ike Zhao League of Suiyuan. The map and geography cannot be arbitrarily fabricated. My army is stationed in Woye because there are few houses in Wulinhe. After negotiating with Yan Xishan, a part of the army is stationed in Woye to avoid freezing to death. The Ning Ma does not allow passage through Ningxia, and Suiyuan's territory does not allow marching. The wilderness is covered with ice and snow, and life is difficult. Isn't this deliberately putting the entire army in a dead end? Who started the trouble? Who is acting barbarously? Who is disregarding justice? I have telegraphed the central government, asking them to send high officials to supervise the departure and investigate the facts. I hope you can report this to He Yingqin and ask him to consider the suffering of tens of thousands of officers and soldiers who have survived the war and are now trapped in a dead end. Telegraphed the central government to quickly send high officials to investigate the truth. I support the central government and have no other intentions. I believe the central government can easily resolve this local matter with an order." (21st Dispatch) (Nanjing) Regarding the Sun-Ma conflict, since the telegram ordered the cessation of military actions and ordered Sun to stop advancing west, peace has been established on the front, and a part of Sun's army has arrived at Woye via Suiyuan and intends to advance towards Ma Hongbin's defense area on the east bank of the river. The General Staff of the Military Commission has drafted a plan for dealing with the situation, which will be decided after Chairman Chiang returns to Nanjing. The conflict is expected to be resolved. (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Zhu Shaoliang telegraphed Nanjing on the 19th, stating that he had sent a telegram to Sun Dianying on the 14th, which read: "Commander Sun Dianying of Baotou, I have received your message. After your troops were ordered to stop advancing west, they suddenly launched an attack and occupied Dengkou, which is extremely alarming. You have also declared everywhere that your resorting to arms is only against a certain party and not against the central government. You are using the fallacious view of religious and ethnic interests as a conspiracy to provoke discord. You may think this is enough to deceive the public and facilitate your selfish plans, but you should know that the foreign enemy is pressing hard, and the people of the country are seeking unity to resist the enemy. How can such wild words be allowed to undermine this? Moreover, the Hui people are all part of the nation, have always obeyed the central government, supported the government, and love the country no less than others. How can they be discriminated against? Shao Yun has repeatedly yielded, unwilling to start a conflict in a time of national crisis and make fools of ourselves, giving others a laughingstock. But you have not realized this and continue to press on. Moreover, I have heard that some of your troops are of complex composition and make reactionary propaganda wherever they go. Your actions are not only a clear defiance of orders but also a great violation of public opinion. Therefore, I earnestly and sincerely advise you to consider the future of the country, not to ignore the inner warnings, and to quickly withdraw from Dengkou, leaving everything to be handled by the central government's clear orders. Otherwise, you will be the culprit of this conflict, or it may lead to even greater problems. Not only will the military and civilians of Gansu, Qinghai, and Ningxia be forced to deal with you out of self-defense, but the people of the whole country will disapprove of your actions. If you fail to follow public opinion, success or failure is inevitable. What good can a mere show of force do? Sincerely yours, Zhu Shaoliang, cold." (21st Dispatch)

Mongolian Representatives and Fellow Townsmen in Beijing

Passed Important Resolutions Yesterday 34

Submit to the Central Government that the Autonomous Method Cannot be Accepted

Request the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee to Revoke the Resolution of the Central Political Council

If There is Still No Result, All Will Leave Beijing Together

Huang Shaoxiong Issues a Statement 35

(Nanjing) Mongolian League and Banner representatives and representatives stationed in Beijing held a temporary talk meeting for fellow townsmen in Beijing on the afternoon of the 21st, with over a hundred people attending. They decided: 1. Submit to the Central Government that they cannot accept the autonomous method decided by the Central Political Council, and notify the compatriots across the country. 2. Regarding the aspects of the Central Political Council's decision on the autonomous method that do not conform to the Mongolian situation, submit them to the Central Government and notify the compatriots across the country. 3. Announce the circumstances under which Minister Huang accepted the eleven articles of the autonomous method in Bailingmiao and the review by the central authorities. 4. Send a letter to Minister Huang asking him to state whether he accepts the eleven articles of the Bailingmiao autonomous plan in order to clarify his responsibility. 5. Send a letter to President Dai, stating that he should take responsibility for the errors in the review of the autonomous plan as an important matter. 6. Request the Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Executive Committee and Chairman Chiang to revoke the autonomous method decided by the Central Political Council this time, and promptly implement the original plan agreed upon in Bailingmiao. If there is still no result, the following methods will be adopted: 1. All representatives to Beijing will return to Mongolia and request punishment. 2. All representatives stationed in Beijing will resign from their original positions and return to Mongolia immediately. 3. All Mongolian personnel and students in Beijing will return to Mongolia. 4. Since the method allowed by Minister Huang is equivalent to zero, the original claim of Bailingmiao should be restored, and the local autonomous government should be organized by Mongolians themselves in order to unite and resist the enemy and avoid becoming a sequel to Eastern Mongolia. Yang Fen and others were appointed on the spot to assist the representatives in carrying out everything. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Mongolian representative Sulu Yun stated that the representatives who came to Beijing have expressed their inability to accept the Mongolian autonomous method passed by the Political Council. In addition to requesting assistance after Chiang Kai-shek arrives in Beijing, they also plan to issue a denial letter and declaration within days, seeking fair criticism from the people of the country. In addition, Yu Youren, the president of the Supervisory Yuan, expressed sympathy for the demands of the Mongolian people and agreed to submit them to the Fourth Plenary Session for discussion in order to comfort the Mongolian people. (21st Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Recently, the Inner Mongolian representatives in Beijing have had many misunderstandings about the plan decided by the Central Government. The reporter visited Huang Shaoxiong to inquire about the truth. His statement is recorded as follows: "Many people outside believe that I was ordered to participate in the Inner Mongolian Autonomous Conference and sign various conditions, but they do not know that the Inner Mongolian Autonomous Conference was an automatic conference of Mongolians, and there was no need for central personnel to participate. When I arrived in Bailingmiao, the conference had already closed. Only its presidium reported the progress of the conference and its demands to the Central Government. Regarding the Inner Mongolian request for autonomy, I can only answer the principles allowed by the Central Government. As for the detailed methods, the Central Government will naturally consider the circumstances of all parties and formulate, announce, and implement them. This is the highest decision-making power of the central government and cannot be determined by dispatched personnel or local personnel. Recently, Inner Mongolian representatives have had misunderstandings about the Central Government's final decision, and they do not seem to understand the above-mentioned reasons, and they are also unclear about the handling process. Because recently, Inner Mongolian representatives have also asked in writing whether I accept the eleven articles drafted by the Mongolian side in Bailingmiao. After receiving this letter, I felt very strange. Why did the representatives who came to Beijing this time and the previous representatives stationed in Beijing who had personally witnessed the process in Bailingmiao unanimously raise questions? It is very incomprehensible. The Inner Mongolian inspection report has been submitted to the Central Political Council. Because the text and materials still need to be supplemented and sorted out, it has not been published. In order to enable the representatives who have come to Beijing and people from all walks of life to understand the truth, the handling process will be selectively published first to dispel doubts. On November 10, I arrived at Bailing. On the 12th, Yun Wang, De Wang, and others sent more than 30 articles of the autonomous government organization law in the name of the presidium, requesting that they be submitted to the Central Government for record. I believed that it was too far from the Central Government's intention, and there was no need to discuss it. I did not agree to submit it and planned to return the original documents and return to Beijing to report. Later, after Yun Wang, De Wang, and others came to explain that it was a document sent to the Central Government and me for reference, I stayed to discuss it further. On the 13th, I talked with Yun Wang and De Wang about the autonomous issue. I believed that the Inner Mongolia's self-organization of the autonomous government had the risk of destroying the country's entire organization and affecting international relations, and the Central Government would never allow it. I instructed them to accept the Central Government's plan to set up local government affairs committees in separate provinces. At that time, Yun Wang did not express anything, while De Wang repeatedly stated the necessity and reasons for Inner Mongolia to organize an autonomous government. On the 14th, we talked again. De Wang still insisted on the entire autonomous government organization. I agreed that on top of the provincial organization, a joint meeting could be held once a year or two to facilitate communication. On the 15th, I made slight additions and deletions based on the plan set by the Central Government and attached practical issues. On the 16th, Yun Wang and De Wang sent representatives Bao Yueqing, Sulu Dai, and others to discuss and study together with representatives Li Songfeng, He Yangling, Kong Qingzong, and others. The representatives of Yun Wang and De Wang put forward eleven articles, the first of which still requested that Inner Mongolia set up a unified highest autonomous organ, and the other articles were also related to the first article. I immediately refused to discuss it. On the 17th, I ordered the entourage to prepare to return to Sui and ordered the entourage to return the documents. On that day, the representatives asked to stay for one more day, guaranteeing a satisfactory solution. At 12:00 PM, Yun Wang and De Wang sent Kang Ren and other representatives to submit their final written requests for two methods, A and B. On the 18th, Yun Wang and De Wang came to ask for instructions. I believed that Method A was still in line with the principles set by the Central Government and agreed to submit it to the Central Government for approval and implementation. Yun Wang and De Wang both expressed satisfaction and sent a Hao telegram (on the 19th) to express their gratitude. On the 19th, I set off to return to Sui. This is the outline of the handling process. In short, what I allowed to be submitted to the Central Government in Bailingmiao was Method A, which they put forward later, and not the eleven articles. However, the Inner Mongolian representatives in Beijing often claimed that they overthrew the eleven articles decided, but they did not mention the six items of Method A, which Yun Wang and De Wang finally requested in writing. It is very puzzling. As for the eleven principles set by the Central Government, they are roughly the same as the items in the final decision of Bailingmiao, and the various feasible issues in the eleven articles that were not decided in Bailingmiao were also selectively adopted." At this point, Huang showed the document finally submitted by Yun Wang, De Wang, et al. and the eleven articles of the Mongolian proposal that were not allowed to be submitted, as follows: Method A: ㈠ Name: Defined as the Mongolian First Autonomous Region Government, the Mongolian Second Autonomous Region Government, and so on. ㈡ Region: The Silingol League and the Chahar Ministry's banners are compiled into the Mongolian First Autonomous Region Government, the Ulanqab League and the Alxa Ejina banners are compiled into the Mongolian Second Autonomous Region Government, and other leagues and banners are compiled into districts according to the proportion. ㈢ Affiliation: The Mongolian Autonomous Region Governments are directly under the Executive Yuan. In the event of an event involving the province, the provincial government will consult on the method. ㈣ Powers: The Mongolian Autonomous Region Governments manage all government affairs of all leagues and banners within their respective regions. ㈤ Funding: The funding for the Mongolian Autonomous Region Governments is issued by the Central Government on a monthly basis. ㈥ Liaison: A joint meeting is set up between the Mongolian Autonomous Regions to discuss common matters between the autonomous regions. Method B: A unified highest autonomous organ of Mongolia is established, named the Mongolian Autonomous Committee, which is directly under the Executive Yuan and manages all government affairs of all leagues and banners. Its funding is allocated by the Central Government on a monthly basis. The original text of the eleven articles proposed by Mongolia but not allowed (omitted). (21st Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) Zhangjiakou telegram: Buyindatige, Guo Mao, Han Fenglin, and other representatives sent to Beijing by De Wang of the Xilingol League arrived at Pangjiang from De Wang's residence, planning to go to Beijing via Zhangjiakou. Bao Yueqing, the former representative of the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Conference, came to Zhangjiakou from Beiping on the same day and immediately telegraphed Wulanqab, stating that the Central Government had deleted the eleven articles decided by Huang Shaoxiong in Bailingmiao, so the three representatives decided to return to Pangjiang for the time being and wait for further reports, but there has been no news of them coming south. (21st Dispatch)

Chahar Eastern Incident

Negotiations Have Come to a Head 36

The Japanese Side Claims It Was a Misunderstanding in Suppressing Bandits

On the One Hand, They Make Unreasonable Demands Again

A Large Number of Korean People Arrive in Guyuan

Japanese Troops Reconnoiter the Situation for Days

(Beiping) After the Japanese army in Eastern Chahar attacked Zhao Jiaying outside Longmensuo again, after Huang sent Liu Shisun and Qin Dechun to negotiate with the Japanese Embassy, the Japanese military officer Shibayama received a telegram from Nishiyi, the commander of the 8th Division, stating that the Japanese army entered outside Longmensuo due to a misunderstanding in suppressing bandits and has now withdrawn to Heihe, hoping that the Chahar authorities will not increase troops to Eastern Chahar. Passing Important Resolutions

League of Nations Administrative Council Closes 53

Appointing a Three-Member Committee

To Study the Methods of the Saar Plebiscite

Passing the Opium Report 54

Representative Gu Eloquently States the Scourge of Narcotics in the Four Northeastern Provinces

(Geneva) Before the conclusion of the 78th session of the League of Nations Council, several extremely important events were considered and passed by the Council. The most significant of these was the decision on the methods for organizing the Saar region's self-determination vote next year. The matter was first presented by Mr. Arroxy, the League of Nations' special inspector for the Saar issue, who suggested that the Council should begin preparations for the issue immediately. Arroxy also advocated forming a small committee of three members. In addition to himself, he should be one of the members, and two other members of the Council should be appointed as members. Their task would be to study the Saar issue and report on how to conduct the vote. The report should be submitted at the Council's meeting in mid-May of this year. The Council expressed its agreement with Arroxy's suggestion and appointed Spanish representative Madaliaga and Argentinian representative Catillo to form a small committee with Arroxy and prepare a report. This report should include the following three items: 1) Studying the necessary methods to ensure that the people's self-determination vote is completed in a correct and lawful manner. 2) Considering what methods to use to protect the people's safety, so that they are not subject to any pressure or coercion from any party to interfere with the freedom of voting. 3) Deciding what steps should be taken to maintain law and order in the Saar region during the self-determination vote process. (National News, 20th)

(Geneva) Today, the League of Nations Administrative Council unanimously passed a resolution on the Saar issue, stating that the League of Nations is determined to guarantee the freedom, secrecy, and accuracy of the plebiscite in the Saar region. A committee composed of Italian representative Arroxy and the representatives of Spain and Argentina is now studying methods for an orderly plebiscite, with particular emphasis on protecting the people from coercion. With the business of the Administrative Council completed, politicians are leaving here tonight. The British delegation is the first to depart for home. (Reuters, 20th)

(Geneva) Today, the League of Nations appointed special commissioners Mr. Arroxy, Mr. Medaliaga, and Mr. Gandhilo to specifically investigate the Saar region issue. 1) Investigate the election matters in the area. 2) Investigate the security of residents in the area. 3) Study the suggestions of the region's administrative committee regarding protecting the area and securing the people. Mr. Pengu said that this special committee is very important because there may be riots when the people of the Saar vote. (National News, 21st)

The Saar Issue 55

Pengu Explains Three Points Should Be Noted

(Geneva) The Administrative Council of the League of Nations unanimously decided to appoint Italian representative Arroxy, Spanish representative Madagaliaga, and Argentine representative Gandilo to form a committee to submit a report on the methods of the Saar plebiscite. Arroxy proposed that the committee study various methods so that, when the Saar citizens vote, they can express their intentions freely and secretly in good conscience, without being subject to any threats, and that measures should be taken to maintain order during the voting period. This proposal was also passed by the entire body. French Foreign Minister Pengu explained that France is involved in the Saar issue, on the one hand, in the capacity of a party concerned, and on the other hand, as a member of the League of Nations. The reason why it is a party concerned is that the Treaty of Versailles stipulates that the Saar has the possibility of merging with France. However, the reason why France is concerned about the Saar issue is mostly because France is a member of the League of Nations. Because it has an obligation to guarantee the people's right to self-determination, not only France, but all members of the Administrative Council should find ways to ensure that the Saar vote is held in accordance with the law. There are three points that should be noted: 1) Protect the people of the Saar so that they can vote freely in good conscience. 2) Guarantee voters from mistreatment after the event, just as we have already granted guarantees to officials. 3) In addition, there is also the maintenance of order during the preparation of the vote, which should also be maintained. Since the League of Nations is the trustee of the Saar's sovereignty, the Administrative Council should find ways to arrange all of these things. (Reuters, 20th)

The Opium Issue 56

The Narcotics Scourge in Puppet Manchuria Harms the Whole World

The Report Explains There Are Triple Dangers

(Geneva) Dr. Gu Weijun delivered a speech at the League of Nations Administrative Council today, first describing the opium situation in China, and then saying that the establishment of an opium monopoly in Manchuria is sufficient to hinder the League of Nations' efforts to eliminate drugs. The Chinese government is particularly willing to provide the League of Nations with all relevant information that can be collected regarding the import of narcotics into Manchuria and Jehol. He greatly supports the opinion of the Opium Advisory Committee, namely that the countries producing and manufacturing the drugs should be asked to pay extremely strict attention to the applications for that region. Dr. Gu also said that the establishment of an opium state monopoly in Manchuria and Jehol is purely for profit and that the organized efforts to promote its production and consumption not only endanger the happiness of the Chinese people but may also harm all countries. The report of the Opium Advisory Committee stated that the committee had carefully considered the new phenomenon of Manchuria, also known as "Manchukuo," and believed that there are triple dangers in the area, namely: 1) In a place where opium production and consumption have already been excessive, the status of opium and other dangerous drugs has become more serious. 2) Persian soil has been imported into an area already full of drugs. 3) If the authorities do not plan appropriate measures to prevent the establishment of secret drug factories, the harm will not only affect China but also other countries. The report also mentioned that the smuggling of cocaine into India, which had decreased at some times, has recently increased greatly, and smugglers are using various new methods of transportation, even using private planes. The Administrative Council debated the report of the Opium Advisory Committee for a long time, and finally passed the report. (Reuters, 20th)

(Geneva) The opium issue has been resolved amicably today. When the League of Nations Administrative Council held an open meeting, Chinese representative Dr. Gu Weijun stated that he was pleased to announce that China had ratified the Opium Limitation Convention. Gu also stated that Manchuria and Jehol are still under foreign military occupation, and the situation of opium and narcotics in that area gives the Opium Advisory Committee legitimate reasons for anxiety. (Reuters, 20th)

The Bolivia-Paraguay Dispute 57

The Investigation Team's Report is Passed

The Representatives of the Two Countries Engage in Heated Debate at the Meeting

(Geneva) The Saar issue has been decided by the Administrative Council of the League of Nations. This matter has at least come to an end within the current session of the Administrative Council. The Administrative Council then continued to discuss the conflict between Bolivia and Paraguay. The League of Nations sent a committee to South America to investigate the situation on the ground. The situation reported by the committee as of January 12th is that since the two countries have now resumed war, the investigation team cannot continue negotiations without receiving new instructions from the Administrative Council. The representative of Bolivia said that the League of Nations investigation team is commendable for fulfilling its mission with a bright attitude. The representative of Paraguay said that Bolivia's desire to extend the truce agreement is intended to take advantage of the opportunity to reorganize its troops in order to attack again. The Bolivian representative stood up to reply, and the Argentine representative also expressed his opinion. At this point, all the items on the Administrative Council's agenda had been discussed, and the 78th session was adjourned. (Havas, 20th)

Japan and Germany Owe the League of Nations Fees 58

The Committee on Current Expenses Will Submit for Discussion

(Geneva) When the League of Nations' Committee on Current Expenses discusses income and expenditure tomorrow, there will be a detailed discussion on the arrears owed by Germany and Japan. Germany and Japan are still required to pay membership fees and maintain the expenses of the League of Nations' new office within two years of withdrawing from the League of Nations. It is deeply believed here that both Germany and Japan will fulfill their obligations and pay the full amount. Recently, the League of Nations Secretariat received 600,000 Swiss francs from Germany, which is half of the pledged donation from 1932. It has been said that membership fees and other expenses will be paid soon. Japan's annual fee of 1,967,253 Swiss francs is now overdue, but Japanese representatives have stated that Japan will clear all debts, and the overdue annual fee will also be paid soon. The committee will also consider in detail the requests from small South American countries to reduce their annual fees. According to League of Nations experts, although Germany has not participated in League of Nations meetings, it has paid its annual fees, while the South American countries have participated in various affairs but have never paid. If Germany and Japan clear their debts this time, then they will necessarily demand that the South American countries repay their historical arrears. If their arrears are tolerated, then Britain will also stop paying in September of this year. Britain pays 3,466,499 Swiss francs to the League of Nations each year, accounting for most of the League of Nations' total current income, so it has a great influence on the League of Nations. (National News, 21st)

Leaves Room for Continued Negotiations 59

(Paris) According to what is revealed in the morning newspaper here, Germany's reply to the French memorandum still leaves room for continued negotiations. Furthermore, Germany does not attach importance to the possibility of France reducing its military aircraft by 50%, because Germany itself has no air force. The morning newspaper further stated that the German reply requested the French government to clarify the points that were not clearly stated in its memorandum. This is a delaying tactic by the German government to resolve the disarmament issue. The Little Parisian newspaper stated that the content of the German reply is extremely complex and very difficult to analyze. The document not only contains requests for further explanations but also contains extremely strict observations and counter-proposals. Therefore, it is impossible to judge whether continued negotiations are possible without carefully reviewing it. (National News, 20th)

Hirota Strives

To Break the Diplomatic Stalemate 65

Wait Until Manchuria is Successfully Managed Before Settling Accounts with Russia

Russia Emphasizes Concluding a Non-Aggression Treaty, Japan Emphasizes Resolving Outstanding Issues

Demonstrations in Front of the Russian Embassy in Japan

The Puppet State Changes its System, Dreaming of Recognition from Various Countries

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that re-opening the war against Russia will frustrate the policy towards Manchuria. Before the management of Manchuria is successful, war must be avoided. Foreign Minister Hirota has met with the Russian ambassador several times, and his purpose is to seek a new path for breaking the deadlock in Japanese-Russian diplomacy. Foreign Minister Hirota agreed to release the Russian workers as a condition for re-opening the illegal negotiations on the Chinese Eastern Railway, intending to break the new situation. According to the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov's policy towards Japan still emphasizes the conclusion of a non-aggression treaty first, but Japan still insists on starting with resolving outstanding issues. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs' policy towards Russia is as follows: 1) First resolve the Chinese Eastern Railway issue, sweep away Russian political and economic forces from the entire territory of Manchuria. 2) Each of the Japanese, puppet, and Russian borders should designate 50 miles as a non-garrison area, using the non-militarized zone policy as a means to avoid war and maintain peace between the three countries. 3) Organize a border committee of Japan, Russia, and the puppet state to demarcate the border and handle local disputes between the three countries. 4) The Red Army must withdraw from the Russian territory in the Far East. 5) The Russian fisheries rights, oil issues, and forest issues must be resolved together. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs' policy towards Russia is the opposite of Russia's policy towards Japan, and the military department does not fully believe in Foreign Minister Hirota's diplomatic policy. There are slight differences in the claims of both sides, and the future is still not optimistic. (Chinese United News, 21st)

The empire believes that this is sufficient to increase [Manchukuo]'s prestige as a new country in East Asia and consolidate the foundation of independence, and sincerely welcomes it. 2) I hope that all countries will frankly recognize this new fact that exists in East Asia in order to adjust international relations with Japan and [Manchukuo]. The Parliament Reopens Tomorrow

The Japanese Political War Begins 66

The Seiyukai and Minseito Hold Party Conventions Separately

Both Speak of Upholding Parliamentary Politics

(Tokyo) The Parliament reopens on the 23rd. Today, the Seiyukai convened a party convention. President Suzuki delivered a speech as follows: Withdrawing from the League of Nations, [Manchuria]'s independence, etc., Japan is facing extraordinary times both internally and externally. However, it is very dangerous to be confused by the calls for extraordinary times and follow foreign countries. We should base ourselves on traditional patriotism and economic strength and always implement national policies with an independent attitude. Politics, diplomacy, national defense, etc., are all organs of the entire country, and not exclusively owned by politicians and soldiers. Therefore, we should pay attention to this point and formulate national policies. Therefore, last year our party decided on the outline of national policies and submitted it to Prime Minister Saito. What kind of sincerity does the government have to implement it? You can fully examine it in parliament, but you should always be based on the country. Recently, there has often been discussion about political institutions, doubts about parliamentary politics, and welcoming the lawlessness of dictatorship, which is deeply regrettable. Japan's parliamentary politics can be seen clearly by looking at the Meiji Restoration's imperial decree. Its origin is in the past of the imperial ancestors, and today it is the duty of the people to complete constitutional politics. The theory of dissolving political parties is also misleading. Political parties have been organized for decades. Although there may be criticism during this period, we cannot but admonish each other to improve parliamentary politics. (Electrical News, 21st)

(Tokyo) The Minseito held a party convention this afternoon. More than 3,500 people attended. US House of Representatives Passes with Absolute Majority

Roosevelt's Currency Bill 69

Amendments All Rejected 70

Equalization Fund to Become a Permanent System

Financial Circles Express Willingness to Cooperate with the Government

(Washington) Today, the House of Representatives ratified President Roosevelt's previous actions regarding currency. By a vote of 360 to 40, it passed the currency bill to devalue the dollar and establish an equalization fund. All opposition was defeated. Various proposals from the authorities were quickly approved by the majority Democrats, while several amendments proposed by the Republicans were rejected. The currency bill is currently under review by the Senate Banking Committee and is expected to pass, possibly becoming law around January 23rd. Meanwhile, pro-silver factions in the Senate have drafted amendments aimed at raising the price of silver. (Reuters, 20th)

(Washington) Although the Secretary of the Treasury has had his first talks with the presidents of the Federal Reserve Banks, and it is reported that the presidents have agreed to cooperate, the dollar devaluation plan is now facing severe criticism from the House of Representatives. Several amendments are currently pending, which may prolong the House debate. However, both Democratic and Republican leaders believe that President Roosevelt will secure a majority vote. Two of President Roosevelt's most trusted expert advisors will attend to answer various criticisms. It is expected that Professors Warren and Rogers will be able to overcome the opposition. The House of Representatives convened an hour earlier. Democratic leader Barnes warned the House not to leave their seats until the currency bill is passed. At the same time, Representative Somers, Chairman of the House Coinage Committee, stated today that President Roosevelt does not want the life of the equalization fund to be subject to time constraints. From this, it seems that the fund will become a permanent institution. (Reuters, 22nd)

(Xuzhou) Zhang Zhenhan, commander of the 41st Division, has come to Xuzhou from his defense post in Xiangyang. He has scheduled the funeral for his mother for the 26th and will bury her at the foot of Yunlong Mountain. The cemetery will be built in the style of a park, open for sightseeing, to adorn the famous mountain. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Bandit Activity Underway in Northern Huai 79

(Qingjiangpu) According to a circular issued by the Huai River Northern Tax Verification Branch Office to Lishui, Guanyun, and other counties, bandit leaders Pan Lianmiao and Shi Bintian, among others, have recently gathered hundreds of followers, carrying multiple handheld machine guns and Mauser pistols. They are lying dormant in the Dayishan, Wangji, Yangji, Longgou, Zhangdian, and Xinanzhen areas, engaging in covert activities and plotting wrongdoing. In addition to dispatching customs enforcement units to search and suppress them, orders have been issued to strictly strengthen defenses, pay attention to reconnaissance, and prevent the spread of unrest. (Special Dispatch, 21st)

Clerk of Jiangyin Party Headquarters Detained 80
