Random Scolding 245

— Ni Shuohan

There is also a kind of dissatisfaction with critics, saying that so-called critics like to [randomly scold], so their writing is not criticism.

This [random scolding] is written as [漫駡] by some people, and [謾駡] by others. I don't know if they have the same meaning. But let's put that aside for now. The question now is what is [random scolding]?

If you point at a person and say: This is a prostitute! If she is a respectable woman, then that is random scolding; if she is really making a living by selling laughter, then it is not random scolding, but telling the truth. Poets don't buy official titles, and the rich only know how to calculate, because that's the way things are, so this is the truth. Even if it is called random scolding, the poet still can't buy a title. This is a small nail where fantasy meets reality.

Having money does not necessarily mean having talent, understanding the nature of children is not necessarily clearer than [having a houseful of children]. [Having a houseful of children] can only prove that the couple is good at giving birth and knows how to raise them, but it does not mean that they can talk nonsense about children's rights. To talk about it is just shameless. This seems like random scolding, but it is not. If you say it is, you have to admit that all the child psychologists in the world are the parents who are best at having children.

Saying that children will fight for a little food is wronging children, in fact it is random scolding. Children's behavior comes from nature, and also changes due to the environment, so Kong Rong would let his pear go. Those who fight are influenced by the family. Aren't there also adults who fight for family property and seize inheritance? The children learned the way.

Random scolding has wronged many good people, but vaguely extinguishing [random scolding] protects all bad seeds.

Fragments of Travel 246

— Liu Ming

If we say that the happiness of travel lies in constantly seeing new scenery and getting new stimuli, then in terms of the border areas of China, traveling in western Yunnan is the most fortunate. Of course, there is one condition that must be added, that is, not to encounter bandits robbing on the road.

The reason why traveling in western Yunnan is so interesting and unforgettable is that the climate in some places will show the different states of two countries in one day's journey, and the life in some places will also mark out two centuries in one day's journey. different phenomena.

I remember that the year I went to Myanmar from Kunming, around the second month of the lunar calendar, when I passed through Lefeng County, I saw broad bean flowers blooming and rape flowers turning green in the fields outside the city in the morning. It was a good time in mid-spring, and the climate was also very mild. After turning over a few mountains, at noon, when I arrived at a place called Xiaowa (surrounded by high mountains, with small valleys in the middle), it was as if I had arrived in another country. The broad bean leaves were already yellow and old, and they were being harvested by farmers. The sun was scorching hot, just like the beginning of May. The trees around were also lush green, without any spring weather at all. When I rested in front of someone's house and asked for water, the dog was too lazy to bark, lying on the wall, panting. People were bare-backed, sleeping on cool mats, enjoying the happiness of a midsummer nap. The sound of flies filled the house, showing the unique scenery of hot weather. In the evening, when I arrived at Shezi, although the fields were gradually covered with the hazy night, the fragrance of spring flowers and the smell of wild grass could still be smelled. It makes people feel as if the spring that disappeared at noon has returned again in the evening.

In Lefeng City at night, every shop has a stinky oil lamp, but on Shezi Street, it is only a day's journey away. Lamps, shops are simply as rare as phoenix feathers and unicorn horns. Not to mention the use of kerosene lamps, even the use of sesame oil lamps is extremely rare. Well, in this way, it seems that people on Shezi Street close their doors and go to sleep at night, and do no business at all. No, on the contrary, the evening is still lively, and the street is brightly lit. This is because every shop or household nails an iron plate on the wall and puts small strips of pine wood (that is, pine wood containing a large amount of rosin) on it, lighting a small ball of raging fire to illuminate the entire room. Walking on the street, smelling the fragrance of pine smoke and looking at such a strange scene, recalling the mood of ancient times, it lightly rippled in the heart of the traveler.

Live Pig Raft 247

— He Jiahuai

The raft was untied.

As if slipping away, the raft drifted effortlessly downstream; except for turns or shallow waters where a bamboo pole was needed, it barely required any human effort.

The water was a deep green. Snow fell on it, light as goose feathers touching the ground, unheard. Yet, as it melted, bubbles appeared. If you looked closely, you could see their round shape, like tiny fish spitting froth from the bottom.

On the high mountains on both sides, the snow had piled up thick. It was dazzlingly white, its fresh luster undimmed even by the gloomy sky.

Three live pig rafts were linked together, one after the other, drifting like lines on the deep green water.

The pigs squealed fiercely, threatened by the cold. The pigpens were covered only by a bamboo screen. All sides were open. Except for a few rough fir timbers, there was no barrier. Snow easily drifted onto them. And they had nothing to eat, hungry all day, so they squealed shrilly, constantly gnawing at the fir timbers. "These beasts deserve to die!"

The old raftsman said resentfully, his brow furrowed, as if he had never heard a pig squeal before. He wore a bamboo hat, a worn raincoat, and a pair of long, large leather boots that reached above his thighs, almost covering his entire trousers.

"I hate live pigs. If it were ham, that would be great. Not to mention anything else, you could eat your fill!"

Then he began to ramble about the time he poled a ham raft, tired of eating ham, even throwing fatty meat into the water. He said that as long as your stomach could hold it, you could eat half a leg in one meal, and the ham merchant wouldn't say a word. And the ham raft only had the fatty, greasy aroma, absolutely none of the headache-inducing pig squeals and pig manure smell.

That manure smell was truly unbearable. Even on that clear, vast river, the pungent odor remained, as if you had locked countless fertilizer-soaked pigs in a small, unventilated room. "Is this raft yours?"

I suddenly thought to ask.

"No, it belongs to our master."

The raftsman fell silent, turning his head away, fearing I would ask him more. I heard that all the rafts on this river, large or small, belonged to raft owners. The raftsmen had to rent them at high prices, like rickshaw pullers, under very harsh conditions. So, although these raftsmen traveled back and forth on this river regardless of the cold or heat, they still couldn't make a living, let alone support their families.

The raft drifted downstream.

The mountains stretched along both banks, sometimes turning several bends, seeming to break the mountain range, but soon emerging with even more majestic, overlapping peaks.

Villages were scarce in this area, only a few scattered here and there. As our raft passed, many barefoot children ran out of the snow-covered houses to watch because they heard the pig squeals. There were many wooden bridges, one after another.

The snow kept falling, the sky was gray, and our mood was as bleak as the sky. It was New Year's. Instead of staying in a warm home, we had to brave the wind and snow, traveling on this river with these pigs, inevitably feeling a little melancholy.

As dusk approached, the raftsman tied the raft to a withered tree along the shore. On the beach, he chose a relatively dry spot and put up a cloth shed, inside which he spread some rice straw brought with the raft, as a bed.

He started a fire.

But the pigs squealed shrilly, gnawing at the fir timbers, and the pig manure smell spread in the darkness.

This continued until the next morning, when the raft was untied again...

The Problem of Muslims Not Eating Pork 248

— Ma Yiyuan

I have experienced not eating pork, and I have felt the aversion to pork. My maternal grandfather was very knowledgeable about Islamic philosophy, and he often advised people to "recognize the True Master and sincerely aspire to goodness," not valuing those who merely perform rituals and pretend to be virtuous. When I was young, one day I went to the street with him and met someone carrying a string of pork coming towards us. I hurriedly pulled him away, saying:

"Grandpa! Quick, let it pass!"

"What?" he asked calmly.

"The pork is coming!"

"What does it matter? Why are you making such a fuss?"

It turned out that we Chinese Muslims not only don't eat pork, but even touching it is taboo. Clothes that have been touched by pork can only be worn normally after washing, and cannot be worn to the mosque for worship. I remember when I was young, I used to fight with non-Muslim children, and I felt quite brave, but as soon as I saw the opponent holding a piece of lard and chasing after me, I would be defeated without a fight! My grandfather only advocated not eating pork, and naturally he didn't deliberately touch it. If he accidentally touched a pig or pork, he also thought he had touched something unclean, but it could be washed away; he didn't need to avoid seeing pork as if it were a ghost. At that time, I didn't quite understand him, and I only heard the general Ah Hong (i.e., religious leader) say that he was "not good at teaching," and was a "heretic." Although the dark shadow of my faith has now been removed by the light of modern knowledge, I am always particularly interested in issues related to Islam or Muslims, and I often want to stand on the position of respecting other people's beliefs and contribute some opinions on habits that should be improved. At the same time, I also want to provide some research data for people who study sociology and religion. This article can be considered a starting point.

I have thoroughly checked the recently translated Quran and English and French translations, and they only contain articles prohibiting eating pork and do not mention any other taboos against pigs. Even the main text of the Chinese Islamic Canon only has two articles: "Do not eat the pig" and "Pig filth." Only in the Q&A in the annotations is there such a question and answer: "If that is the case, is it enough to abstain from eating it? Why bother to avoid contact with the fishy and greasy, and hate it as an enemy? Answer: This is the meaning of preventing slight deviations and stopping them at the beginning. It cannot be otherwise."

Whether the opinions in the annotations are unique to China, I have not been able to find out for the time being, but the following three conversations with Muslims from other countries can be used for everyone's reference.

The first time I went to Marseille for business, I took the time to visit a secretary in the Egyptian consulate who was a Muslim. After I explained the purpose of my visit, he expressed his welcome, and we began the following questions:

"Islam prohibits eating pork. Does it also prohibit touching pigs or pork?"

"No, the prohibition of eating is clearly stipulated in the Quran. Of course, if touching causes pollution, it should be washed."

"Do you cook your own meals here, or do you eat in ordinary restaurants?"

"Naturally, I go to restaurants to eat. Pork is more expensive than beef in Europe. If I want a plate of veal, they will never replace it with pork. We can rest assured."

"Our country's Muslims also prohibit touching pigs or pork. If clothes are touched, even after washing, they cannot be worn again during worship. Is this in accordance with scripture?"

"As far as I know, the Quran only has regulations on abstinence from eating. I dare not say anything else. But I know that there is an Egyptian Muslim who has made the pilgrimage to Mecca three times, and he should have more religious knowledge than me, and his business is raising pigs, raising them and selling them to Europeans. Then how can he avoid touching the pigs he raises? I think perhaps it is enough not to eat them."

"Can you tell me the reason for the prohibition of eating?"

"This is probably because pigs are too dirty and poisonous. Moreover, we live in the tropics..."

(To be continued)

Father and Daughter (3) 249

— Jin Yi

But Mother Xiang never came back after all, and Father had been saying the same words for three, five, ten years!

During these days, she saw white hair grow on her father's head because of sorrow; her father's health also deteriorated because of excessive drinking. She thought that besides reminiscing about the woman he loved, her father was also thinking that his daughter would soon follow the man she loved and leave. Then he would be left alone, living out his remaining years in solitude. So she told her father that she would absolutely not abandon him.

"Is that so, is that so?"

Father looked at her with doubtful eyes, but his voice was trembling for some reason.

"I'm not saying anything false or exaggerated."

She remembered how firmly she looked at her father's face at that time, and how extraordinary she looked.

"I don't want to ruin my daughter's youth for my sake."

"But I am willing to exchange my youth for my father's happy days, but there is one thing," she paused, "I don't want my father to indulge in alcohol anymore, it will harm your health!"

"I promise you, child."

So they hugged, and she felt her father's hot tears flowing on her neck, and she herself shed tears.

In this way, they spent a year of peaceful and beautiful days. She often pretended to be a child, wanting her father to forget his old age: she carefully served him, as considerate as a loyal lover. Father was often so moved that he seemed to have something to say, but she immediately interrupted him, not wanting him to continue, but saying herself:

"I am your daughter, all these things are what I should do."

But recently, Father has been haunted by that old melancholy again. He didn't say it clearly, maybe he thought in his heart that this was a bit unfair to his daughter; but he couldn't restrain himself; when he was suffering from the memories of the past, he would naturally look at the portrait hanging on the wall. In his eyes, it was not just a stiff portrait, but something that could laugh and talk with his thoughts. He remembered how her smile had two lovely dimples, and when she spoke, people could see how beautiful her teeth were. He also remembered that there was a crimson mole at the corner of her eye, but it was not in this portrait, because it was covered by her hair. He could still remember everything she had said, those empty words, and when he remembered them, it was as if she was whispering in his ear again. Now all this was gone, and only by recalling could a clear shadow flash through his mind.

The grown-up daughter had the same beautiful face as her mother, and such a good heart. He knew that his daughter's heart was good, better than her mother's, and better than all women's. Every time he thought this way, he could increase his belief in forgetting that heartless woman; but because of his daughter, he could also easily think of his daughter's mother. He often wanted to sit there alone, or take a walk, so that the old affection could be revived in his own heart. He wanted to avoid his daughter, because he knew that this was somewhat unfair to her.

That night, they sat there silently until fatigue made their eyes feel dry and their heads drooped slightly.

"Dad, go to sleep, it's getting late."

"Is it?"

He raised his eyes and looked at the clock hanging on the wall, it was already 11:25.

"Really, it's almost twelve o'clock, I still feel like it's only been a while."

She said this deliberately, but in fact, that night, she felt like a year had passed!

"Okay, let's go to sleep, let's go to sleep."

Inner Mongolia Autonomy 250

— Geng

Our country's national character and vitality were insufficiently cultivated from the beginning, and not enough effort was made to restore them afterward, resulting in a country with a hundred holes and a thousand sores, a sick man. After a carbuncle on his back just healed, his belly started bleeding again, attracting countless large green-headed flies, buzzing around him, waiting for a chance to choose a fatty spot and bite! This old man [sick man] and his body are constantly being bitten, even forming new sores that are about to fester. If the rest of his body doesn't help drive away the flies or assist with salvarsan 606 and 914, is it likely that the whole body will be bitten to death by the flies, one part at a time? It's like a rotten boat in a huge, turbulent wave. Everyone is working together to patch the cracks, still fearing that the dangerous situation cannot be sustained and that the treacherous shoals cannot be crossed. If everyone still harbors ulterior motives and private views, secretly and openly trying to flirt with a huge warship sailing head-on—a warship that will crush the broken boat, seize jade and silk, and eat flesh and blood—do you think the people in this boat are the kind who are "wearing official hats but fleeing towards death"?

Reports say that the Central Political Council has passed eleven articles on Inner Mongolia's autonomous rule. They certainly sound reasonable. However, thinking back to the fate of its elder brother—Outer Mongolia, which has now disappeared without a trace—it also started with a grand and imposing autonomy. Moreover, Inner Mongolia's increasingly intense demands for autonomy come after the great pain of losing the Northeast and at a time when the puppet organization is about to change its name to "Manchukuo" and has already invaded Chahar East, occupying Zhaojiayingzi (all reported in the newspaper on the 18th). The passage of those eleven articles has caused our startled and fearful hearts and our thoughts after the pain to arouse a hot, stinging sensation, as if thinking with pain: "That rabbit is probably about to leave that burrow!"

But the world is so big, strange things are truly endless. As mentioned above, at this time of serious national crisis, when we should be helping each other in the same boat, the passage of those eleven articles on autonomy already feels like an unfortunate and excessive product! Unexpectedly, Inner Mongolia's league and banner representatives, Zhao Taibao and fourteen others, still thought it was not enough and went directly to the Central Political Council to petition for maintaining Minister Huang's original plan negotiated at Bailingmiao, that is, to further increase the powers of the autonomous region government (see the newspaper on the 19th), "otherwise we will absolutely not dare to accept it and will only return to Mongolia with tears of blood, awaiting slaughter." How urgent their desire for autonomy is, and how determined they are to oppose the review proposal is something we should not ignore. Reading their petition, the tone seems very much like a man in Qi who has a wife and a concubine. Unfortunately, his family fortune has declined, his wife has secretly fled with her lover, and his concubine wants a divorce but cannot get it, and he can't help but say resentfully: "My wife secretly fled, you have no say! Now my concubine formally proposes economic independence, no, formally seeks a peaceful divorce with you, but you hinder and doubt her, why are you so unappreciative?" Can this kind of vile tone not make people hate them to death?

Ought to be the Task 251

— Zu

It was probably four or five years ago, it was a summer day, it was two days before the summer vacation, it was the summer when I graduated from junior high school, the term exams were over, and I was already more than half happy, especially after I found out that my score was passing, that was even more indescribably happy. So I gathered a large group of classmates and went to talk to a certain teacher, and sit with a certain Mr. Wang. Mr. Wang's small room was completely occupied by our large group of classmates. Mr. Wang suddenly asked me: "Zu, are you planning to go to high school?" "I am planning to go to high school," I replied simply. "I suggest you go to a mission school." To be a slave to a conquered country, to be a running dog? It is better to go to a national or provincial school." Mr. Xu arrogantly corrected Mr. Wang's weakness. Actually, young people living in the world today is really extremely difficult, those without money to study can continue to study, secretly shedding tears, and those who have prepared money to study are still facing difficulties everywhere, and finally [fluent English] and supporting, overthrowing, and holding meetings cannot solve the question of bread for young people."

Like mission schools, which prohibit students from free activities in the school, even if there are any meetings, the teachers order them to be carried out rigidly. The establishment of this ×× entertainment meeting at our school today is completely student-initiated. The school is completely in the position of an observer, so this spirit is respectable and lovely ..."

After he finished speaking, a slight wave rose in my heart, and a nameless shadow floated up. It is said that this ×× entertainment meeting was cultivated by sacrificing the entire precious study time of many students. A school is a small society. In addition to reading dead books, of course, I do not object to various extracurricular activities in the school, but the so-called extracurricular activities should also have considerable limits. If they do some kind of ghost tricks at will, as long as the location is within the school, it is considered an extracurricular activity in the school, which is always very ridiculous. But I always believe that when they are young, in addition to being lively, they should also be guided to develop good reading habits, which is the task that teachers should do.

Don't Just Laugh at Others 252

— Where to Go

Westerners worship God, Indians worship the Great God, Muslims worship the Living Buddha, and Chinese people worship their ancestors. Regardless of whether this God, Great God, Living Buddha, or Ancestor is dead or alive, fictitious or real, has an idol or does not have an idol, in short, they are all kinds of idol worship, all kinds of seeking help from the superhuman divine power that may or may not exist to solve their own problems in real life when they encounter difficulties. There is no distinction between superior and inferior in this.

Some people believe in God, and then laugh at Muslims, saying that their kind of worship is foolish and absurd. This is just like Chinese people laughing at Westerners for worshipping God, and worshippers of God laughing at Chinese people for worshipping their ancestors, which is equally ridiculous.

Watching the performance of the funny character in the theater is certainly funny, but those laughing audiences may not be funny themselves. People who hold lettuce and bite it while mocking those who bite live fish are not necessarily truly clever, nor are they necessarily more civilized than the latter.

People always feel that their own is good. People wearing Western suits laugh at those wearing robes, and people wearing robes laugh at those wearing Western suits. But looking at it coldly, which is not ridiculous?

Fortune and Fate 253

— Qiong Sheng

In the current economic crisis that is deepening day by day, the "fate" of the general public, if they do not rise up and actively control it themselves; then "fate" will control you, destined to be swept by the tide of panic below the starvation line, which is already "undoubtedly" without needing to consult the tortoise shell. But many people do not understand this, wanting to become "lucky ones" amidst the agitation of the entire society's masses tending towards poverty, bankruptcy, suicide, and being killed. Therefore, they fast and bathe, pray to gods and worship Buddha, hoping to have the "God of Wealth and Bodhisattva" come under the protection of the divine sky. This kind of phenomenon at the end of society is enough to express the general public's passive attitude of "unsurpassed resentment" towards the status quo, but it is also their cowardly mentality of hoping for luck and living in peace. This kind of cowardly mentality, just like monks and nuns taking advantage of it to consolidate God's "will" while making a lot of money for themselves, is also used by social rulers to chant "national prosperity" and "national future" as spells, while making a fortune for themselves. This is the biggest of them. As for the wind of superiors and subordinates following suit, shops, companies, and restaurants also use "hope for × million yuan" to attract customers, practicing their road to wealth of "losing money and restraining themselves," it is as numerous as books and cannot be detailed.

Therefore, we can win prizes by smoking cigarettes now, we can win prizes by washing soap, and recently we can even win prizes by eating soup dumplings at Risheng Building on Nanjing Road. If you spend ten Sun Yat-sen silver dollars to "enthusiastically save the country," you can hope to become a millionaire worth 500,000 yuan, which is even more well-known. This shows that although our China is the poorest country in the world, the "God of Wealth and Bodhisattva" are everywhere, as long as your "ancestors have virtue," you can have the shining of a lucky star. But according to a report from the National News Agency on the 13th: the United States is also planning to imitate our country's method and has decided to issue national lottery tickets, which makes us feel even more "our path is not lonely."

After Roosevelt took office in the United States with the slogans of saving the crisis and relieving unemployment, there was a lot of noise, White House talks, London conferences, currency inflation, and industrial recovery, and again and again, he found a "magic pill" to treat the incurable disease of the capitalist system. But some things go against people's wishes. Although the Eagle flag flutters throughout the country, until now, almost a year has passed, and the number of unemployed people is still more than 10 million, the market still does not see how prosperous it is, and in the context of currency inflation and rising prices, the market has shrunk instead, and the so-called industrial recovery in the United States is even more "vague." Therefore, Roosevelt, the god of fate of this Yankee race, is becoming increasingly exhausted, gradually losing his faith under the disappointment of the people's desire to "find work and eat bread." Therefore, the clever Roosevelt came up with a plan of "golden cicada shedding its shell" to prevent the general public's despair about saving the crisis and relieving unemployment from being blamed on himself, and in the struggle of hunger, he gave them the opportunity to get rich - issuing national lottery tickets. Thus, thousands and tens of thousands of unemployed people groaning in hunger and cold clench their stomachs and wait for the arrival of "fortune," no longer taking risks and entering the path of extremism, the country is peaceful, and the world is fine. Therefore, the so-called "national" "revival" ×× lottery ticket wind is prevalent for a time. In the current situation where the broad masses of the people are mired in extreme poverty, it does not come out of the following two meanings:

First, the economic crisis and the unemployment and poverty of the people are caused by the imperfection of the social and economic system,

Second, the people are blessed by unemployment and bankruptcy, and almost nothing can be scraped from them in the form of direct taxes and indirect taxes, except for their bare hands.

Here we may as well repeatedly remind those who hope that "fortune" will come to be vigilant. At this time when the economic crisis is sweeping the world, your "fate" has been decided by the mountains, either to shed a few more drops of sweat and tears for the "nation and people," or to serve the "motherland" on the battlefield as cannon fodder. The so-called national lottery tickets and what lottery tickets are just "sleeping pills" to guide you on this path, if you do not bravely rise up and control your own "fate."

Carving Out a Path to Survival! 254

— Tian Zhuzi

In this day and age, there are two kinds of people who can make a living: first, the sons of wealthy capitalists and old gentry; second, those who gamble, run brothels, speculate, or open banks. Anything else is simply too difficult to survive! Open a factory or a store? Heavy taxes, difficulty in collecting debts, troublesome employees, and exorbitant rent: managing to scrape by is the best outcome; closing down and going bankrupt is no cause for complaint. This is indeed the current state of China, so opening a factory or a store is not "good business." Go to school? Not to mention primary and secondary schools, even graduating from university and finding a six-yuan-a-month internship is not easy. Moreover, studying requires capital, unlike the old days of "rising from humble beginnings" and "commoners becoming officials." If your family has connections and influence, you can hold onto two, three, four, or five...rice bowls, otherwise, no matter how talented and knowledgeable you are, no one will seek your advice, and you won't even be allowed to hold onto half a rice bowl. Therefore, studying is also not "good business." Work as a clerk and eat someone else's rice? First, you need connections, and with a recommendation, you also need a guarantor. Once the recommendation and guarantee are settled, you also need to understand the art of dealing with people, diligence and patience are essential; knowing how to flatter is even more essential. If you adhere to the old moral code, with its principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, you are guaranteed to face obstacles and be hindered at every turn. The new era has new morals. Can those who are well-versed in ethics textbooks adapt to modern society? Therefore, working as a clerk and eating someone else's rice is also not "good business." So, what is this so-called "good business"? I believe that to carve out a bloody path in this dark and bewildering life journey, one must quickly emulate Columbus, the explorer of the New World!

The cries of modern youth are filled with a gloomy and miserable atmosphere. All publications are filled with these cries of misery. In reality, this is fundamentally wrong! If you were to file a complaint on the street, would the gentlemen and ladies in their cars jump out to help you? Filing a complaint with robbers is no different! Will these impoverished scholars' meager writings ever catch the eye of the gentlemen and ladies? Therefore, instead of writing these essays in vain, it is better to discover a new land for yourself.

Page 20

Jia Changsha's tearful articles and Qu Lingjun's wandering by the riverbank not only failed to move the hearts of rulers, but even drowning oneself in the Miluo River would be a "wrongful death"!

How to find a new land for yourself? To use a gambler's term: it's called "betting on a long shot." While everyone is rushing to the cities, I will rush to the countryside. Although the rural areas are bankrupt, there are still many things that can be done: animal husbandry, planting trees, and trading. Moreover, rural life is less expensive, with plenty of sunshine, good air, and relatively kind people. One can drink wine and tend to hemp, not caring about governance and chaos. There are many things to do in the countryside. Is there only one path to take—the cities? Having said that, it's not like the cities are impossible to go to. First, choosing a career requires caution and careful consideration. If the "true meaning of life" lies in making money, then, if you cannot follow the wealthy old men in the cities, you must associate with idle friends. It all depends on the individual's ingenuity, and it is not difficult to "shake" yourself up one day. Otherwise, carrying an old goods pole or running a few stalls, being diligent and thrifty, you still won't starve. Otherwise, cheating, swindling, stealing, looting, selling daughters as dancers, actresses, or "salted meat," sons picking up cigarette butts, pulling yellow cattle across bridges, robbing pimps, skinning pigs, taking bribes, or running gambling dens are all enough to make you a "master" in Shanghai. These are all "long shots" and new lands discovered by Columbus!

Enough with the idle talk, let's get back to the main topic. Although the universe is narrow, there is still a place to eat. Do not blindly follow the crowd and sink into despair. You should use your brain a little and "bet on a long shot." Filing complaints in publications is useless. At the same time, why don't the editors of various publications put the valuable space to better use by publishing more novel and practical articles on small businesses and small crafts, so that the youth who are wandering on the wrong path can carve out a path to survival? Wouldn't that be more beneficial?

Selling Smiles 255

— Qu Chen

"Selling smiles" usually refers to prostitutes who provide entertainment with their bodies, but the actual meaning is no longer encompassed by these two words. However, it is also used in its original sense. On December 27th of last year, a news item appeared in the newspaper as follows:

London, World News Agency: Miss Petans Panlin is a woman who earns her living by "smiling" for the whole world. She fears that her beautiful smile may one day fade, so she has insured her smile for 1,000 pounds. She must smile fifty times a week, allowing various newspapers and magazines to capture her image. She recently told someone: "My smile is my most precious property and cannot be lost, so I have insured it for 1,000 pounds. Sometimes I get tired of smiling, so I just get in my car, disappear for dozens of days, and then return."

Upon first reading this news, it seems that Miss Petans Panlin must be extraordinarily noble, with a smile worth insuring for 1,000 pounds. But upon closer thought, the situation is quite tragic.

Smiling is the ultimate expression of emotion and must be heartfelt, that is, unintentional. Whether you "smile gently" or "laugh uncontrollably," there is always an underlying reason why you cannot help but smile. We cannot force someone who wants to cry to sing, just as we cannot force someone who wants to sing to cry. When smiling becomes "acting," it completely loses the meaning of "smiling" and is actually close to crying, or even worse. The common saying "selling smiles by the door" is only the observation of the host. From the perspective of the "seller," it should be "tears" and "blood." Laughter before a feast often turns into tears on the pillow. How often can a trace of true joy be found in the world of pleasure? Using the blood and tears of others for one's own laughter is a cruelty that humanity has always engaged in. Miss Petans Panlin's pride only makes her more pitiful.

But then again, earning a "living" by "smiling" is ultimately an easy and welcome thing, as long as you don't think of yourself as a person, a person with independent dignity. People who serve the gentlemen and ladies day and night, taking their joys and sorrows as their own, are "born in this world" and can be found everywhere. It's not just Miss Petans Panlin's unique behavior. These people, like Miss Petans Panlin, proudly regard their "smile" as their "most precious property," fearing its loss, but are completely unaware of their pitiful state. This kind of "selling" should be distinguished from the "selling smiles" of prostitutes who are forced into a life of prostitution due to social persecution.

Mary's Freedom (3) 257

— Man Zhi

You said again based on my words:

"I can't ruin him by letting him continue to degenerate like this. It's better for me to leave him!"

"You want to leave? Where will you go?" I was so surprised!

"I'll go back to my mother's place, but I'm someone who ran away from a marriage, and I don't want to go back! I'm a lonely person, and even if I want to leave him, there's no path for me to take!..." You said, and burst into tears!

You are truly pitiful, but how can I comfort you? Can I encourage you to seek an independent life? I can't. Because Renjie is my friend, and he loves you. My words of comfort at the time were so irrelevant. I said,

"Renjie is just acting differently recently, he is a good and promising young man, you shouldn't leave him, if you leave him, you will only ruin him more, he will not know how far he will degenerate!"

You were silent. I also felt that there was nothing to say.

Before long, Renjie returned. He was still so dejected, and at the same time, he was complaining. When I brought up his decadence and disregard for life, he denied it with heroic spirit. I could only sarcastically say that it was good that he wasn't degenerating.

A few days later, he ran to my place, laughing wildly as soon as he entered the door. This was naturally "abnormal," and I was very surprised and worried. I was worried because you must have left him. I knew you had left him, but I didn't tell him. If I had told him first, he might have changed his behavior and confessed to you and gained your understanding. Wouldn't that have been okay? Wouldn't that have prevented him from going so crazy? I regretted it. This was my fault! But it was too late. You had left him, and he was crazy! God, I am a sinner!

He laughed wildly for a long time before saying this:

"My Mary, she, left me, she's gone!"

Saying that, he laughed again, fell back on the chair, his bloodshot eyes staring at the ceiling. Suddenly, without warning, he stood up from the chair, grabbed my collar with both hands, and shouted,

"Look, is our life destined to be a tragedy?"

I sympathized with his situation, and his words struck a chord in my heart. I, too, was acting out a tragedy on the road of life! How could I comfort him at that time? I was the one who needed comfort!

"There's no way out for us, our thoughts are bitten by poisonous snakes, our emotions are like a volcano erupting, but even our loved ones can't give me a little comfort, we," he cried miserably, "are we already on the path to the grave? Are we destined to commit suicide?"

Besides hugging him and comforting him, what words could I use to comfort him?

"No, no!" he cried again, "We are not weak, we are not bastards, we have to catch up with the times, we have to die for meaningful sacrifices, we cannot commit suicide; suicide is the act of the weak, suicide is a shameful act!... Women, women, women are devils! But..." his voice became faint and weak again, "I love her, I can't live a day without her! Look, she is so beautiful and gentle, and her attitude is so generous. Who among our girlfriends can compare to her..." At this time, I helped him to the lotus throne and gave him a glass of water to drink 重I said

"Opening the　　　　　　　　　the same　isn't　a joke?"

Unexpectedly, his face changed immediately, the fire of anger burned in his bloodshot eyes, and he said to me fiercely.

A Visit with Chinese Film Artists (34) (Continued from Yesterday) 258

— Sha Ji

(XIV) "Struggle" Director Shi Dongshan (Part 2)

"In the current situation, do you have any opinions on political matters?" I asked. "I feel that no matter what the political environment, we should always criticize and denounce political errors and social ills from the standpoint of a citizen. Of course, films should be related to politics, but forcing films to become the mouthpiece of politics is ultimately a very foolish method. Because it is ultimately impossible. Unless the film artists themselves feel deeply satisfied with a certain political ideology."

"Then what kind of films do you think China needs at present?" I asked again. "Of course, I am not satisfied with the current society, so I think there is a great need for films that expose social contradictions. Naturally, this must be proven by facts. I personally oppose films that only expose without giving any direction. We should make the audience become the driving force for promoting society after watching the film. It is very clear that society has problems, and the people themselves also have problems. For example, we blame non-resistance, but we should also show the power of resistance ourselves. Many people often like to sit alone and make sarcastic remarks, which is a very wrong attitude..."

He said many other things here, which need not be recorded one by one. Then I said;

"Now what I want to know is your opinion on world cinema."

"Humph, this is a big topic. But simply put, I think the recent Russian films are indeed very powerful in propaganda. Their films are not just something fun. British films have made great progress in recent years. American films have a few writers who are struggling hard in their consciousness, striving to improve. German films have been scarce recently, with no new ideas. In short, the films of all countries are striving to raise their own status, but Chinese films do not recognize their great power, which is really a pity."

"To say another sentence, film must change with social changes, and film must become what the audience needs."

Speaking of this, I asked him about his future film production plans. His answer was that social and national issues are equally important, because both are urgently needed at present. For example, this film "Woman" deals with social issues, and the next film will deal with national issues. Then I asked;

"Since you entered the film industry, how many films have you made?"

"Let me think about it." He said: "...Humph, it's twelve in total."

"Among them, can you list the important ones that you consider satisfactory?"

"This..." he said in the tone of a Beijing opera recitation.

"Homosexual Love"丨丨 1925 (24 years old)

"Children and Grandchildren's Fortune"丨丨丨 1926

"Four Heroes of the Wang Family"丨丨 1926

"Extraordinary Woman"丨丨丨 1928

"Hengniang"丨丨丨丨 1930

"Struggle"丨丨丨丨 1932 (31 years old)

Finally, I asked him about his experience in entering the film industry. His answer was;

"I was originally a person who studied painting, and I often went to the ChunGuang Art Association. Later, because I was friends with Dan Duyu, I became an actor in the Shanghai Film Company, but it was actually just an amateur role. This was when I was twenty years old. Because I was able to draw, I occasionally drew a few title backgrounds, and gradually became involved in set design and so on. Until I was twenty-three years old, I began to direct a film called "Yanghua Hen," which starred the so-called 'flirty sister' Han Yunzhen... The rest can be omitted."

The conversation ended here, and there is no need to record other idle talk in detail. On this day, we talked about social news and even national affairs, until about one o'clock in the afternoon, before braving the heavy snow to go home. (End of XIV)

Film Reviews

Review of "Exhibition" 259

— Ling He

丨Produced by Star, Premiered at XinGuang丨

"Exhibition" is largely adapted from "The Lin Family Shop," which is a very obvious fact. Of course, we do not require the playwright to be completely faithful to the novel, because literature and film have great differences in the creative process. However, "Exhibition" and the original work have completely changed their original essence, especially after the failure of Xie Changyuan's (Lin Family Shop) foreign goods store, plus a section of "promoting domestic products," "exhibitions," etc., which is completely contrary to the entire theme. I think this is the most unwise method. As for the many other places where the original meaning of the original work has been abandoned, that is of course another problem.

Rural bankruptcy, reduced purchasing power, indirect and direct extortion and exploitation, conspiracies and infighting between merchants, unrest in the times, financial panic, merchants' slow turnover, and small capital stores can only face a very miserable bankruptcy. This is the most obvious and inevitable fact. At the same time, it must be clearly written in the original work: "It would be strange if he didn't collapse... The master extorts him, the money shop oppresses him, and the same industry slanders him, and he has to eat bad debts, who can bear such heavy torture?... "

These things are all said in a very obscure way in the film. However, at the end, the playwright suddenly adds an inexplicable tail. The spirit of advocating domestic products with earnestness is commendable, but it is an extremely incomprehensible contradiction in "Exhibition." For example, after Xie Changyuan's bankruptcy, the YongShengXiang family, who had committed many evils, also went bankrupt, saying that it was affected by Xie Changyuan, which is also an unsustainable place. This is completely a cowardly act to cater to the audience's feudal established psychology and to achieve a retribution that is clear to all. Of course, we are not saying that YongShengXiang can still survive in this recession, but in order to make people happy, we cannot say a better reason. But it cannot but make people criticize. Suppose, just after Boss Zhao escaped, his production was auctioned off and shared; wouldn't this tragic ending deepen the stimulation of the merchants more?

We cannot forget the director's method in his considerable success in "Fragrant Grass Beauty." But in this film, he completely failed.

㈠We cannot clearly distinguish which one is YongShengXiang and which one is Xie Changyuan, and sometimes we mistakenly refer to A as B. This reminds us of Warner's "Business," which is also two stores across the street; the difference is too great.

㈡There is no emotion in the play, and even a little melancholy atmosphere is not well grasped. I think this is the place that makes the audience feel the most disappointed.

㈢The sets are too simple and too fake. Snow is made of cotton wool, white powder, and paper scraps. Isn't this intentional to make people sigh?

㈣The actors have no roles to play, especially Sun Min and Wang Mengshi, they are simply a little bit of fine decoration. The better ones are of course Xie Yunqing and Gao Yian. Wang Zhengxin is next, Xia Peizhen is next, as for a man wearing a black velvet mandarin jacket, decorated with a water pipe, who plays the owner of the money shop, it really makes people laugh.

㈤The makeup is too fake, especially the owner of the money shop. Xie Yunqing also has the same problem in several scenes. I really don't understand why he is so careless?

In short, this is a work below the standard line of the Star Company.

In Memory of Mr. Jin Chuansong 260

Mr. Jin Chuansong was a worker in the electrical department of the Lianhua No. 2 Factory, and also an excellent and hardworking technician in our film culture movement. At the end of 1933, when he participated in the film "Song of the Fishermen" directed by Mr. Cai Chusheng, he was accidentally stabbed in the foot by a nail on the photography field, and the wound festered and finally died in the Sports Hospital on January 10 of this year. To commemorate our loss of a loyal comrade, we held a memorial meeting at the Lianhua No. 2 Factory Club on the 14th of this month. At the meeting, we especially expressed our greatest respect for Mr. Jin's spirit of independently helping with work after being injured, and cited it as a model for each of our colleagues in the future. At the same time, it pointed out that only by improving the factory's internal medical equipment and developing the close mutual assistance spirit among colleagues can the recurrence of unfortunate events be reduced. At the same time, in order to commemorate Mr. Jin's great working spirit, it was decided to erect a bronze plaque in the second factory for permanent commemoration. Finally, the colleagues initiated a post-mortem donation to maintain the old age of Mr. Jin's mother, and the various post-mortem measures for Mr. Jin were also entrusted to the service department of the Colleague Association by the General Assembly for proper handling.

Screen Couple Gainor and Farrell to Collaborate Again 261

— A Yun

In the past year, the problem of the non-cooperation of Janet Gaynor and Charles Farrell was a major change that shocked the silver screen, and even Farrell voluntarily terminated the contract and left Fox, and those who had a good impression of them both expressed considerable regret. However, according to the recent formal announcement of Fox, Gainor and Farrell will partner again and continue to cooperate on two films, and a contract has been formally signed. It is indeed a more gratifying fact for movie fans all over the world who have been looking forward to it for a long time. Even Farrell himself wanted to struggle out of a new form and a new self in the re-cooperation. Therefore, before the contract was signed, he specifically put forward a clause that he had the right to accept or reject the script, and it had to conform to his tonality and have a considerable opportunity to act. He will no longer be an appendage of Gainor, and he wants audiences all over the world to understand that he is a member with a rich personality, and he does not rely on Gainor's performance to achieve his fame. The first film began work at the beginning of this month, and the title has not yet been formally announced

Charlie Chaplin and German Chancellor Hitler 262

— Si Ying

An American film magazine said with a humorous tone: Hitler's subordinates will be at odds with Charlie Chaplin, because the little mustache of this comedian is too indistinguishable from the little mustache of Hitler, the leader of the National Socialist Party, the majestic chancellor of Germany. Some people also said that Charlie himself was unwilling to keep that little mustache, because he was afraid of being mistaken for Hitler. Some people also said that the German National Socialist Party has asked Charlie to shave off his little mustache, because his ridiculous little mustache is obviously joking with their leader. But we must know that Charlie's little mustache is not from today. Long before Hitler's name was known, this comedian had already used that little mustache, big boots, and cane as his trademark. According to trademark law, Hitler is still a counterfeit! But it is a very obvious thing that Charlie Chaplin's films may be difficult to enter German territory.

Broadway Through a Keyhole (2) 263

— By Xin Zhi

Judge Li Qi said: [What? Only you deserve that flower, because you yourself are more beautiful than a magnolia. But you haven't seen what's inside the flower yet.] Qiong saw a small package in the middle of the bouquet, and she went to take it. Li Qi quickly stopped her, saying: [Child, don't move it yet, it's not time yet. Wait until you get to your dressing room before opening it.] Qiong smiled coquettishly: [Whatever it is, it's great.] After she finished speaking, she took the flowers back to her dressing room.

Qiong Huilan returned to the dressing room, where Tex was waiting. She unfolded the small package and found a diamond-encrusted bracelet inside. Qiong Huilan exclaimed excitedly: [Tex, come and see, what is this! Judge Li Qi gave it to me! This thing is really beautiful, but of course I can't accept it.] Tex carefully examined the bracelet, then handed it back to Qiong Huilan, saying: [Hey, Qiong, you haven't really made your mark in this kind of place yet, but you have a lot of potential. So I want to tell you, you know people always say that a fool is born every minute in the world, but in fact, it's not like that at all. Fools are rare and hard to find. And, have you ever heard of anyone being poisoned to death by platinum?] After she said that, she stretched out her arm, looked at the bracelets covering her arm, and said: [These things will be very useful when I get older. You have to remember how these things are obtained; it's not by shaking your head from side to side, but by nodding your head up and down.] Now, do you still want to return that bracelet to that guy?] Qiong Huilan said: [Of course, I should return it to him.] Tex shook her head, displaying a look of hopelessness, and walked away.

Qiong Huilan was telling the truth; she said she didn't know Frank Luoqi, who introduced her to this nightclub. Luoqi was a notorious bad guy, and Tex Kalai was also not a good person. Of course, the nightclub she ran was not a reputable place. Qiong Huilan still remembered when she was a child, Frank was a friend of her older sister. At that time, everyone already knew that Frank was a bad kid in the neighborhood. Later, she heard people say that he had joined a gangster group. But she never knew that he had now become the most feared crime boss in New York. What does he do? He is the chairman of a [Chicken and Duck Insurance Association]. All chicken and duck merchants in the New York area must pay Frank Luoqi a protection tax according to the size of their business in order to safely deliver their goods to their customers' homes. Qiong Huilan's older sister, Yiseer, asked him to recommend her younger sister to a theater to study. In Tex's nightclub, Luoqi's words were law, so Qiong Huilan was sent here to work as a singer. One day, Luoqi and his bodyguard Chuck, and Chuck's woman Bierre, came to the nightclub to watch the performance. He gradually noticed the last woman in the row. Tex happened to walk over at this moment. (To be continued)
